 <p><a name="an_37:21">37:21</a> They that render evil for good, have detracted me, because I followed goodness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:22">37:22</a> Forsake me not, O Lord my God : do not thou depart from me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:23">37:23</a> Attend unto my help, O Lord, the God of my salvation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:1">38:1</a> Unto the end, for Idithun himself, a canticle of David. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:2">38:2</a> I said: I will take heed to my ways : that I sin not with my tongue. I have set guard to my mouth, when the sinner stood against me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:3">38:3</a> I was dumb, and was humbled, and kept silence from good things : and my sorrow was renewed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:4">38:4</a> My heart grew hot within me : and in my meditation a fire shall flame out. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:5">38:5</a> I spoke with my tongue : O Lord, make me know my end. And what is the number of my days : that I may know what is wanting to me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:6">38:6</a> Behold thou hast made my days measurable : and my substance is as nothing before thee. And indeed all things are vanity : every man living. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:7">38:7</a> Surely man passeth as an image : yea, and he is disquieted in vain. He storeth up : and he knoweth not for whom he shall gather these things. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:8">38:8</a> And now what is my hope? is it not the Lord? and my substance is with thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:9">38:9</a> Deliver thou me from all my iniquities : thou hast made me a reproach to the fool. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:10">38:10</a> I was dumb, and I opened not my mouth, because thou hast done it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:11">38:11</a> Remove thy scourges from me. The strength of thy hand hath made me faint in rebukes: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:12">38:12</a> thou hast corrected man for iniquity. And thou hast made his soul to waste away like a spider : surely in vain is any man disquieted. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:13">38:13</a> Hear my prayer, O Lord, and my supplication : give ear to my tears. Be not silent : for I am a stranger with thee, and a sojourner as all my fathers were. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:14">38:14</a> O forgive me, that I may be refreshed, before I go hence, and be no more. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:1">39:1</a> Unto the end, a psalm for David himself. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:2">39:2</a> With expectation I have waited for the Lord, and he was attentive to me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:3">39:3</a> And he heard my prayers, and brought me out of the pit of misery and the mire of dregs. And he set my feet upon a rock, and directed my steps. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:4">39:4</a> And he put a new canticle into my mouth, a song to our God. Many shall see, and shall fear : and they shall hope in the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:5">39:5</a> Blessed is the man whose trust is in the name of the Lord; and who hath not had regard to vanities, and lying follies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:6">39:6</a> Thou hast multiplied thy wonderful works, O Lord my God : and in thy thoughts there is no one like to thee. I have declared and I have spoken they are multiplied above number. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:7">39:7</a> Sacrifice and oblation thou didst not desire; but thou hast pierced ears for me. Burnt offering and sin offering thou didst not require : </p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:8">39:8</a> then said I, Behold I come. In the head of the book it is written of me </p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:9">39:9</a> that I should do thy will : O my God, I have desired it, and thy law in the midst of my heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:10">39:10</a> I have declared thy justice in a great church, lo, I will not restrain my lips : O Lord, thou knowest it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:11">39:11</a> I have not hid thy justice within my heart : I have declared thy truth and thy salvation. I have not concealed thy mercy and thy truth from a great council. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:12">39:12</a> Withhold not thou, O Lord, thy tender mercies from me : thy mercy and thy truth have always upheld me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:13">39:13</a> For evils without number have surrounded me; my iniquities have overtaken me, and I was not able to see. They are multiplied above the hairs of my head : and my heart hath forsaken me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:14">39:14</a> Be pleased, O Lord, to deliver me, look down, O Lord, to help me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:15">39:15</a> Let them be confounded and ashamed together, that seek after my soul to take it away. Let them be turned backward and be ashamed that desire evils to me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:16">39:16</a> Let them immediately bear their confusion, that say to me : 'T is well, 't is well. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:17">39:17</a> Let all that seek thee rejoice and be glad in thee : and let such as love thy salvation say always : The Lord be magnified. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:18">39:18</a> But I am a beggar and poor : the Lord is careful for me. Thou art my helper and my protector : O my God, be not slack. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:1">40:1</a> Unto the end, a psalm for David himself. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:2">40:2</a> Blessed is he that understandeth concerning the needy and the poor : the Lord will deliver him in the evil day. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:3">40:3</a> The Lord preserve him and give him life, and make him blessed upon the earth : and deliver him not up to the will of his enemies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:4">40:4</a> The Lord help him on his bed of sorrow : thou hast turned all his couch in his sickness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:5">40:5</a> I said: O Lord, be thou merciful to me : heal my soul, for I have sinned against thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:6">40:6</a> My enemies have spoken evils against me: when shall he die and his name perish? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:7">40:7</a> And if he came in to see me, he spoke vain things : his heart gathered together iniquity to itself. He went out and spoke to the same purpose. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:8">40:8</a> All my enemies whispered together against me : they devised evils to me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:9">40:9</a> They determined against me an unjust word : shall he that sleepeth rise again no more? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:10">40:10</a> For even the man of peace, in whom I trusted, who ate my bread, hath greatly supplanted me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:11">40:11</a> But thou, O Lord, have mercy on me, and raise me up again : and I will requite them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:12">40:12</a> By this I know, that thou hast had a good will for me : because my enemy shall not rejoice over me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:13">40:13</a> But thou hast upheld me by reason of my innocence : and hast established me in thy sight for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:14">40:14</a> Blessed by the Lord the God of Israel from eternity to eternity. So be it. So be it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:1">41:1</a> Unto the end, understanding for the sons of Core. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:2">41:2</a> As the hart panteth after the fountains of water; so my soul panteth after thee, O God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:3">41:3</a> My soul hath thirsted after the strong living God; when shall I come and appear before the face of God? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:4">41:4</a> My tears have been any bread day and night, whilst it is said to me daily : Where is thy God? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:5">41:5</a> These things I remembered, and poured out my soul in me : for I shall go over into the place of the wonderful tabernacle, even to the house of God : With the voice of joy and praise; the noise of one feasting. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:6">41:6</a> Why art thou sad, O my soul? and why dost thou trouble me? Hope in God, for I will still give praise to him : the salvation of my countenance, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:7">41:7</a> and my God. My soul is troubled within myself : therefore will I remember thee from the land of Jordan and Hermoniim, from the little hill. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:8">41:8</a> Deep calleth on deep, at the noise of thy flood-gates. All thy heights and thy billows have passed over me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:9">41:9</a> In the daytime the Lord hath commanded his mercy; and a canticle to him in the night. With me is prayer to the God of my life. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:10">41:10</a> I will say to God : Thou art my support. Why hast thou forgotten me? and why go I mourning, whilst my enemy afflicteth me? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:11">41:11</a> Whilst my bones are broken, my enemies who trouble me have reproached me; Whilst they say to me day be day : Where is thy God? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:12">41:12</a> Why art thou cast down, O my soul? and why dost thou disquiet me? Hope thou in God, for I will still give praise to him : the salvation of my countenance, and my God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:1">42:1</a> A psalm for David. Judge me, O God, and distinguish my cause from the nation that is not holy : deliver me from the unjust and deceitful man. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:2">42:2</a> For thou art God my strength : why hast thou cast me off? and why do I go sorrowful whilst the enemy afflicteth me? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:3">42:3</a> Send forth thy light and thy truth : they have conducted me, and brought me unto thy holy hill, and into thy tabernacles. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:4">42:4</a> And I will go in to the altar of God : to God who giveth joy to my youth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:5">42:5</a> To thee, O God my God, I will give praise upon the harp : why art thou sad, O my soul? and why dost thou disquiet me? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:6">42:6</a> Hope in God, for I will still give praise to him : the salvation of my countenance, and my God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:1">43:1</a> Unto the end, for the sons of Core, to give understanding. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:2">43:2</a> We have heard, O God, with our ears : our fathers have declared to us, The work, thou hast wrought in their days, and in the days of old. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:3">43:3</a> Thy hand destroyed the Gentiles, and thou plantedst them : thou didst afflict the people and cast them out. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:4">43:4</a> For they got not the possession of the land by their own sword : neither did their own arm save them. But thy right hand and thy arm, and the light of thy countenance : because thou wast pleased with them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:5">43:5</a> Thou art thyself my king and my God, who commandest the saving of Jacob. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:6">43:6</a> Through thee we will push down our enemies with the horn : and through thy name we will despise them that rise up against us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:7">43:7</a> For I will not trust in my bow : neither shall my sword save me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:8">43:8</a> But thou hast saved us from them that afflict us : and hast put them to shame that hate us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:9">43:9</a> In God shall we glory all the day long : and in thy name we will give praise for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:10">43:10</a> But now thou hast cast us off, and put us to shame : and thou, O God, wilt not go out with our armies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:11">43:11</a> Thou hast made us turn our back to our enemies : and they that hated us plundered for themselves. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:12">43:12</a> Thou hast given us up like sheep to be eaten : thou hast scattered us among the nations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:13">43:13</a> Thou hast sold thy people for no price : and there was no reckoning in the exchange of them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:14">43:14</a> Thou hast made us a reproach to our neighbours, a scoff and derision to them that are round about us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:15">43:15</a> Thou hast made us a byword among the Gentiles : a shaking of the head among the people. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:16">43:16</a> All the day long my shame is before me : and the confusion of my face hath covered me, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:17">43:17</a> At the voice of him that reproacheth and detracteth me : at the face of the enemy and persecutor. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:18">43:18</a> All these things have come upon us, yet we have not forgotten thee : and we have not done wickedly in they covenant. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:19">43:19</a> And our heart hath not turned back : neither hast thou turned aside our steps from thy way. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:20">43:20</a> For thou hast humbled us in the place of affliction : and the shadow of death hath covered us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:21">43:21</a> If we have forgotten the name of our God, and if we have spread forth our hands to a strange god : </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:22">43:22</a> Shall not God search out these things : for he knoweth the secrets of the heart. Because for thy sake we are killed all the day long : we are counted as sheep for the slaughter. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:23">43:23</a> Arise, why sleepest thou, O Lord? arise, and cast us not off to the end. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:24">43:24</a> Why turnest thou face away? and forgettest our want and our trouble? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:25">43:25</a> For our soul is humbled down to the dust : our belly cleaveth to the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:26">43:26</a> Arise, O Lord, help us and redeem us for thy name's sake. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:1">44:1</a> Unto the end, for them that shall be changed, for the sons of Core, for understanding. A canticle for the Beloved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:2">44:2</a> My heart hath uttered a good word I speak my works to the king; My tongue is the pen of a scrivener that writeth swiftly. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:3">44:3</a> Thou art beautiful above the sons of men: grace is poured abroad in thy lips; therefore hath God blessed thee for ever </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:4">44:4</a> Gird thy sword upon thy thigh, O thou most mighty. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:5">44:5</a> With thy comeliness and thy beauty set out, proceed prosperously, and reign. Because of truth and meekness and justice: and thy right hand shall conduct thee wonderfully. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:6">44:6</a> Thy arrows are sharp: under thee shall people fall, into the hearts of the king's enemies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:7">44:7</a> Thy throne, O God, is for ever and ever: the sceptre of thy kingdom is a sceptre of uprightness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:8">44:8</a> Thou hast loved justice, and hated iniquity: therefore God, thy God, hath anointed thee with the oil of gladness above thy fellows. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:9">44:9</a> Myrrh and stacte and cassia perfume thy garments, from the ivory houses: out of which </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:10">44:10</a> the daughters of kings have delighted thee in thy glory. The queen stood on thy right hand, in gilded clothing; surrounded with variety. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:11">44:11</a> Hearken, O daughter, and see, and incline thy ear: and forget thy people and thy father's house. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:12">44:12</a> And the king shall greatly desire thy beauty; for he is the Lord thy God, and him they shall adore. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:13">44:13</a> And the daughters of Tyre with gifts, yea, all the rich among the people, shall entreat thy countenance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:14">44:14</a> All the glory of the king's daughter is within in golden borders, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:15">44:15</a> clothed round about with varieties. After her shall virgins be brought to the king: her neighbours shall be brought to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:16">44:16</a> They shall be brought with gladness and rejoicing: they shall be brought into the temple of the king. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:17">44:17</a> Instead of thy fathers, sons are born to thee: thou shalt make them princes over all the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:18">44:18</a> They shall remember thy name throughout all generations. Therefore shall people praise thee for ever; yea, for ever and ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:1">45:1</a> Unto the end, for the sons of Core, for the hidden. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:2">45:2</a> Our God is our refuge and strength: a helper in troubles, which have found us exceedingly. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:3">45:3</a> Therefore we will not fear, when the earth shall be troubled; and the mountains shall be removed into the heart of the sea. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:4">45:4</a> Their waters roared and were troubled: the mountains were troubled with his strength. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:5">45:5</a> The stream of the river maketh the city of God joyful: the most High hath sanctified his own tabernacle. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:6">45:6</a> God is in the midst thereof, it shall not be moved: God will help it in the morning early. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:7">45:7</a> Nations were troubled, and kingdoms were bowed down: he uttered his voice, the earth trembled. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:8">45:8</a> The Lord of armies is with us: the God of Jacob is our protector. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:9">45:9</a> Come and behold ye the works of the Lord: what wonders he hath done upon earth, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:10">45:10</a> making wars to cease even to the end of the earth. He shall destroy the bow, and break the weapons: and the shield he shall burn in the fire. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:11">45:11</a> Be still and see that I am God; I will be exalted among the nations, and I will be exalted in the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:12">45:12</a> The Lord of armies is with us: the God of Jacob is our protector. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:1">46:1</a> Unto the end, for the sons of Core. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:2">46:2</a> O clap your hands, all ye nations: shout unto God with the voice of Joy, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:3">46:3</a> For the Lord is high, terrible: a great king over all the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:4">46:4</a> He hath subdued the people under us; and the nations under our feet. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:5">46:5</a> He hath chosen for us his inheritance the beauty of Jacob which he hath loved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:6">46:6</a> God is ascended with jubilee, and the Lord with the sound of trumpet. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:7">46:7</a> Sing praises to our God, sing ye: sing praises to our king, sing ye. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:8">46:8</a> For God is the king of all the earth: sing ye wisely. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:9">46:9</a> God shall reign over the nations: God sitteth on his holy throne. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:10">46:10</a> The princes of the people are gathered together, with the God of Abraham: for the strong gods of the earth are exceedingly exalted. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:1">47:1</a> A psalm of a canticle, for the sons of Core, on the second day of the week. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:2">47:2</a> Great is the Lord, and exceedingly to be praised in the city of our God, in his holy mountain. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:3">47:3</a> With the joy of the whole earth is mount Sion founded, on the sides of the north, the city of the great king. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:4">47:4</a> In her houses shall God be known, when he shall protect her. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:5">47:5</a> For behold the kings of the earth assembled themselves: they gathered together. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:6">47:6</a> So they saw, and they wondered, they were troubled, they were moved: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:7">47:7</a> trembling took hold of them. There were pains as of a woman in labour. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:8">47:8</a> With a vehement wind thou shalt break in pieces the ships of Tharsis. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:9">47:9</a> As we have heard, so have we seen, in the city of the Lord of hosts, in the city of our God: God hath founded it for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:10">47:10</a> We have received thy mercy, O God, in the midst of thy temple. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:11">47:11</a> According to thy name, O God, so also is thy praise unto the ends of the earth: thy right hand is full of justice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:12">47:12</a> Let mount Sion rejoice, and the daughters of Juda be glad; because of thy judgments, O Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:13">47:13</a> Surround Sion, and encompass her: tell ye in her towers. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:14">47:14</a> Set your hearts on her strength; and distribute her houses, that ye may relate it in another generation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:15">47:15</a> For this is God, our God unto eternity, and for ever and ever: he shall rule us for evermore. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:1">48:1</a> Unto the end, a psalm for the sons of Core. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:2">48:2</a> Hear these things, all ye nations: give ear, all ye inhabitants of the world. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:3">48:3</a> All you that are earthborn, and you sons of men: both rich and poor together. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:4">48:4</a> My mouth shall speak wisdom: and the meditation of my heart understanding. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:5">48:5</a> I will incline my ear to a parable; I will open my proposition on the psaltery. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:6">48:6</a> Why shall I fear in the evil day? the iniquity of my heel shall encompass me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:7">48:7</a> They that trust in their own strength, and glory in the multitude of their riches, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:8">48:8</a> No brother can redeem, nor shall man redeem: he shall not give to God his ransom, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:9">48:9</a> Nor the price of the redemption of his soul: and shall labour for ever, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:10">48:10</a> and shall still live unto the end. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:11">48:11</a> He shall not see destruction, when he shall see the wise dying: the senseless and the fool shall perish together: And they shall leave their riches to strangers: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:12">48:12</a> and their sepulchres shall be their houses for ever. Their dwelling places to all generations: they have called their lands by their names. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:13">48:13</a> And man when he was in honour did not understand; he is compared to senseless beasts, and is become like to them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:14">48:14</a> This way of theirs is a stumblingblock to them: and afterwards they shall delight in their mouth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:15">48:15</a> They are laid in hell like sheep: death shall feed upon them. And the just shall have dominion over them in the morning; and their help shall decay in hell from their glory. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:16">48:16</a> But God will redeem my soul from the hand of hell, when he shall receive me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:17">48:17</a> Be not thou afraid, when a man shall be made rich, and when the glory of his house shall be increased. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:18">48:18</a> For when he shall die he shall take nothing away; nor shall his glory descend with him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:19">48:19</a> For in his lifetime his soul will be blessed: and he will praise thee when thou shalt do well to him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:20">48:20</a> He shall go in to the generations of his fathers: and he shall never see light. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:21">48:21</a> Man when he was in honour did not understand: he hath been compared to senseless beasts, and made like to them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:1">49:1</a> A psalm for Asaph. The God of gods, the Lord hath spoken: and he hath called the earth. From the rising of the sun, to the going down thereof: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:2">49:2</a> out of Sion the loveliness of his beauty. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:3">49:3</a> God shall come manifestly: our God shall come, and shall not keep silence. A fire shall burn before him: and a mighty tempest shall be round about him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:4">49:4</a> He shall call heaven from above, and the earth, to judge his people. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:5">49:5</a> Gather ye together his saints to him: who set his covenant before sacrifices. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:6">49:6</a> And the heavens shall declare his justice: for God is judge. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:7">49:7</a> Hear, O my people, and I will speak: O Israel, and I will testify to thee: I am God, thy God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:8">49:8</a> I will not reprove thee for thy sacrifices: and thy burnt offerings are always in my sight. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:9">49:9</a> I will not take calves out of thy house: nor he goats out of thy flocks. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:10">49:10</a> For all the beasts of the woods are mine: the cattle on the hills, and the oxen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:11">49:11</a> I know all the fowls of the air: and with me is the beauty of the field. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:12">49:12</a> If I should be hungry, I would not tell thee: for the world is mine, and the fulness thereof. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:13">49:13</a> Shall I eat the flesh of bullocks? or shall I drink the blood of goats? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:14">49:14</a> Offer to God the sacrifice of praise: and pay thy vows to the most High. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:15">49:15</a> And call upon me in the day of trouble: I will deliver thee, and thou shalt glorify me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:16">49:16</a> But to the sinner God hath said: Why dost thou declare my justices, and take my covenant in thy mouth ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:17">49:17</a> Seeing thou hast hated discipline: and hast cast my words behind thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:18">49:18</a> If thou didst see a thief thou didst run with him: and with adulterers thou hast been a partaker. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:19">49:19</a> Thy mouth hath abounded with evil, and thy tongue framed deceits. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:20">49:20</a> Sitting thou didst speak against thy brother, and didst lay a scandal against thy mother's son: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:21">49:21</a> these things hast thou done, and I was silent. Thou thoughtest unjustly that I should be like to thee: but I will reprove thee, and set before thy face. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:22">49:22</a> Understand these things, you that forget God; lest he snatch you away, and there be none to deliver you. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:23">49:23</a> The sacrifice of praise shall glorify me: and there is the way by which I will shew him the salvation of God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:1">50:1</a> Unto the end, a psalm of David, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:2">50:2</a> when Nathan the prophet came to him after he had sinned with Bethsabee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:3">50:3</a> Have mercy on me, O God, according to thy great mercy. And according to the multitude of thy tender mercies blot out my iniquity. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:4">50:4</a> Wash me yet more from my iniquity, and cleanse me from my sin. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:5">50:5</a> For I know my iniquity, and my sin is always before me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:6">50:6</a> To thee only have I sinned, and have done evil before thee: that thou mayst be justified in thy words and mayst overcome when thou art judged. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:7">50:7</a> For behold I was conceived in iniquities; and in sins did my mother conceive me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:8">50:8</a> For behold thou hast loved truth: the uncertain and hidden things of thy wisdom thou hast made manifest to me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:9">50:9</a> Thou shalt sprinkle me with hyssop, and I shall be cleansed: thou shalt wash me, and I shall be made whiter than snow. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:10">50:10</a> To my hearing thou shalt give joy and gladness: and the bones that have been humbled shall rejoice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:11">50:11</a> Turn away thy face from my sins, and blot out all my iniquities. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:12">50:12</a> Create a clean heart in me, O God: and renew a right spirit within my bowels. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:13">50:13</a> Cast me not away from thy face; and take not thy holy spirit from me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:14">50:14</a> Restore unto me the joy of thy salvation, and strengthen me with a perfect spirit. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:15">50:15</a> I will teach the unjust thy ways: and the wicked shall be converted to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:16">50:16</a> Deliver me from blood, O God, thou God of my salvation: and my tongue shall extol thy justice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:17">50:17</a> O Lord, thou wilt open my lips: and my mouth shall declare thy praise. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:18">50:18</a> For if thou hadst desired sacrifice, I would indeed have given it: with burnt offerings thou wilt not be delighted. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:19">50:19</a> A sacrifice to God is an afflicted spirit: a contrite and humbled heart, O God, thou wilt not despise. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:20">50:20</a> Deal favourably, O Lord, in thy good will with Sion; that the walls of Jerusalem may be built up. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:21">50:21</a> Then shalt thou accept the sacrifice of justice, oblations and whole burnt offerings: then shall they lay calves upon thy altar. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:1">51:1</a> Unto the end, understanding for David, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:2">51:2</a> when Doeg the Edomite came and told Saul David went to the house of Achimelech </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:3">51:3</a> Why dost thou glory in malice, thou that art mighty in iniquity? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:4">51:4</a> All the day long thy tongue hath devised injustice: as a sharp razor, thou hast wrought deceit. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:5">51:5</a> Thou hast loved malice more than goodness: and iniquity rather than to speak righteousness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:6">51:6</a> Thou hast loved all the words of ruin, O deceitful tongue. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:7">51:7</a> Therefore will God destroy thee for ever: he will pluck thee out, and remove thee from thy dwelling place: and thy root out of the land of the living. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:8">51:8</a> The just shall see and fear, and shall laugh at him, and say: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:9">51:9</a> Behold the man that made not God his helper: But trusted in the abundance of his riches: and prevailed in his vanity. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:10">51:10</a> But I, as a fruitful olive tree in the house of God, have hoped in the mercy of God for ever, yea for ever and ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:11">51:11</a> I will praise thee for ever, because thou hast done it: and I will wait on thy name, for it is good in the sight of thy saints. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:1">52:1</a> Unto the end, for Maeleth, understandings to David. The fool said in his hear t: There is no God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:2">52:2</a> They are corrupted, and become abominable in iniquities: there is none that doth good. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:3">52:3</a> God looked down from heaven on the children of men: to see if there were any that did understand, or did seek God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:4">52:4</a> All have gone aside, they are become unprofitable together, there is none that doth good, no not one. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:5">52:5</a> Shall not all the workers of iniquity know, who eat up my people as they eat bread? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:6">52:6</a> They have not called upon God: there have they trembled for fear, where there was no fear. For God hath scattered the bones of them that please men: they have been confounded, because God hath despised them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:7">52:7</a> Who will give out of Sion the salvation of Israel? when God shall bring back the captivity of his people, Jacob shall rejoice, and Israel shall be glad. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:1">53:1</a> Unto the end, In verses, understanding for David. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:2">53:2</a> When the men of Ziph had come and said to Saul: Is not David hidden with us? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:3">53:3</a> Save me, O God, by thy name, and judge me in thy strength. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:4">53:4</a> O God, hear my prayer: give ear to the words of my mouth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:5">53:5</a> For strangers have risen up against me; and the mighty have sought after my soul: and they have not set God before their eyes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:6">53:6</a> For behold God is my helper: and the Lord is the protector of my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:7">53:7</a> Turn back the evils upon my enemies; and cut them off in thy truth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:8">53:8</a> I will freely sacrifice to thee, and will give praise, O God, to thy name: because it is good: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:9">53:9</a> For thou hast delivered me out of all trouble: and my eye hath looked down upon my enemies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:1">54:1</a> Unto the end, in verses, understanding for David. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:2">54:2</a> Hear, O God, my prayer, and despise not my supplication: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:3">54:3</a> be attentive to me and hear me. I am grieved in my exercise; and am troubled, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:4">54:4</a> at the voice of the enemy, and at the tribulation of the sinner. For they have cast iniquities upon me: and in wrath they were troublesome to me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:5">54:5</a> My heart is troubled within me: and the fear of death is fallen upon me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:6">54:6</a> Fear and trembling are come upon me: and darkness hath covered me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:7">54:7</a> And I said: Who will give me wings like a dove, and I will fly and be at rest? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:8">54:8</a> Lo, I have gone far off flying away; and I abode in the wilderness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:9">54:9</a> I waited for him that hath saved me from pusillanimity of spirit, and a storm. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:10">54:10</a> Cast down, O Lord, and divide their tongues; for I have seen iniquity and contradiction in the city. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:11">54:11</a> Day and night shall iniquity surround it upon its walls: and in the midst thereof are labour, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:12">54:12</a> and injustice. And usury and deceit have not departed from its streets. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:13">54:13</a> For if my enemy had reviled me, I would verily have borne with it. And if he that hated me had spoken great things against me, I would perhaps have hidden myself from him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:14">54:14</a> But thou a man of one mind, my guide, and my familiar, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:15">54:15</a> Who didst take sweetmeats together with me: in the house of God we walked with consent. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:16">54:16</a> Let death come upon them, and let them go down alive into hell. For there is wickedness in their dwellings: in the midst of them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:17">54:17</a> But I have cried to God: and the Lord will save me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:18">54:18</a> Evening and morning, and at noon I will speak and declare: and he shall hear my voice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:19">54:19</a> He shall redeem my soul in peace from them that draw near to me: for among many they were with me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:20">54:20</a> God shall hear, and the Eternal shall humble them. For there is no change with them, and they have not feared God: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:21">54:21</a> he hath stretched forth his hand to repay. They have defiled his covenant, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:22">54:22</a> they are divided by the wrath Of his countenance, and his heart hath drawn near. His words are smoother than oil, and the same are darts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:23">54:23</a> Cast thy care upon the Lord, and he shall sustain thee: he shall not suffer the just to waver for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:24">54:24</a> But thou, O God, shalt bring them down into the pit of destruction. Bloody and deceitful men shall not live out half their days; but I will trust in thee, O Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:1">55:1</a> Unto the end, for a people that is removed at a distance from the sanctuary for David, for an inscription of a title (or pillar ) when the Philistines held him in Geth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:2">55:2</a> Have mercy on me, O God, for man hath trodden me under foot; all the day long he hath afflicted me fighting against me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:3">55:3</a> My enemies have trodden on me all the day long; for they are many that make war against me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:4">55:4</a> From the height of the day I shall fear: but I will trust in thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:5">55:5</a> In God I will praise my words, in God I have put my trust: I will not fear what flesh can do against me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:6">55:6</a> All the day long they detested my words: all their thoughts were against me unto evil. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:7">55:7</a> They will dwell and hide themselves: they will watch my heel. As they have waited for my soul, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:8">55:8</a> for nothing shalt thou save them: in thy anger thou shalt break the people in pieces, O God, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:9">55:9</a> I have declared to thee my life: thou hast set my tears in thy sight, As also in thy promise. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:10">55:10</a> Then shall my enemies be turned back. In what day soever I shall call upon thee, behold I know thou art my God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:11">55:11</a> In God will I praise the word, in the Lord will I praise his speech. In God have I hoped, I will not fear what man can do to me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:12">55:12</a> In me, O God, are vows to thee, which I will pay, praises to thee: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:13">55:13</a> Because thou hast delivered my soul from death, my feet from falling: that I may please in the sight of God, in the light of the living. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:1">56:1</a> Unto the end, destroy not, for David, for an inscription of a title, when he fled from Saul into the cave </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:2">56:2</a> Have mercy on me, O God, have mercy on me: for my soul trusteth in thee. And in the shadow of thy wings will I hope, until iniquity pass away. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:3">56:3</a> I will cry to God the most High; to God who hath done good to me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:4">56:4</a> He hath sent from heaven and delivered me: he hath made them a reproach that trod upon me. God hath sent his mercy and his truth, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:5">56:5</a> and he hath delivered my soul from the midst of the young lions. I slept troubled. The sons of men, whose teeth are weapons and arrows, and their tongue a sharp sword. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:6">56:6</a> Be thou exalted, O God, above the heavens, and thy glory above all the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:7">56:7</a> They prepared a snare for my feet; and they bowed down my soul. They dug a pit before my face, and they are fallen into it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:8">56:8</a> My heart is ready, O God, my heart is ready: I will Sing, and rehearse a psalm. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:9">56:9</a> Arise, O my glory, arise psaltery and harp: I will arise early. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:10">56:10</a> I will give praise to thee, O Lord, among the people: I will sing a psalm to thee among the nations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:11">56:11</a> For thy mercy is magnified even to the heavens: and thy truth unto the clouds. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:12">56:12</a> Be thou exalted, O God, above the l heavens: and thy glory above all the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:1">57:1</a> Unto the end, destroy not, for David, for an inscription of a title. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:2">57:2</a> If in very deed you speak justice: judge right things, ye sons of men. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:3">57:3</a> For in your heart you work iniquity: your hands forge injustice in the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:4">57:4</a> The wicked are alienated from the womb; they have gone astray from the womb: they have spoken false things. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:5">57:5</a> Their madness is according to the likeness of a serpent: like the deaf asp that stoppeth her ears: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:6">57:6</a> Which will not hear the voice of the charmers; nor of the wizard that charmeth wisely. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:7">57:7</a> God shall break in pieces their teeth in their mouth: the Lord shall break the grinders of the lions. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:8">57:8</a> They shall come to nothing, like water running down; he hath bent his bow till they be weakened. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:9">57:9</a> Like wax that melteth they shall be taken away: fire hath fallen on them, and they shall not see the sun. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:10">57:10</a> Before your thorns could know the brier; he swalloweth them up, as alive, in his wrath. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:11">57:11</a> The just shall rejoice when he shall see the revenge: he shall wash his hands in the blood of the sinner. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:12">57:12</a> And man shall say: If indeed there be fruit to the just: there is indeed a God that judgeth them on the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:1">58:1</a> Unto the end, destroy not, for David for an inscription of It title, when Saul sent and watched his house to kill him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:2">58:2</a> Deliver me from my enemies, O my God; and defend me from them that rise up against me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:3">58:3</a> Deliver me from them that work iniquity, and save me from bloody men. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:4">58:4</a> For behold they have caught my soul: the mighty have rushed in upon me: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:5">58:5</a> Neither is it my iniquity, nor my sin, O Lord: without iniquity have I run, and directed my steps. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:6">58:6</a> Rise up thou to meet me, and behold: even thou, O Lord, the God of hosts, the God of Israel. Attend to visit all the nations: have no mercy on all them that work iniquity. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:7">58:7</a> They shall return at evening, and shall suffer hunger like dogs: and shall go round about the city. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:8">58:8</a> Behold they shall speak with their mouth, and a sword is in their lips: for who, say they, hath heard us ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:9">58:9</a> But thou, O Lord, shalt laugh at them: thou shalt bring all the nations to nothing. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:10">58:10</a> I will keep my strength to thee: for thou art my protector: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:11">58:11</a> my God, his mercy shall prevent me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:12">58:12</a> God shall let me see over my enemies: slay them not, lest at any time my people forget. Scatter them by thy power; and bring them down, O Lord, my protector: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:13">58:13</a> For the sin of their mouth, and the word of their lips: and let them be taken in their pride. And for their cursing and lying they shall be talked of, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:14">58:14</a> when they are consumed: when they are consumed by thy wrath, and they shall be no more. And they shall know that God will rule Jacob, and all the ends of the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:15">58:15</a> They shall return at evening and shall suffer hunger like dogs: and shall go round about the city. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:16">58:16</a> They shall be scattered abroad to eat, and shall murmur if they be not filled. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:17">58:17</a> But I will sing thy strength: and will extol thy mercy in the morning. For thou art become my support, and my refuge, in the day of my trouble. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:18">58:18</a> Unto thee, O my helper, will I sing, for thou art God my defence: my God my mercy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:1">59:1</a> Unto the end, for them that shall be changed, for the inscription of a title, to David himself, for doctrine, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:2">59:2</a> when he set fire to Mesopotamia of Syria and Sobal and Joab returned and slew of Edom, in the vale of the saltpits, twelve thousand men. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:3">59:3</a> O God, thou hast cast us off, and hast destroyed us; thou hast been angry, and hast had mercy on us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:4">59:4</a> Thou hast moved the earth, and hast troubled it: heal thou the breaches thereof, for it has been moved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:5">59:5</a> Thou hast shewn thy people hard things; thou hast made us drink wine of sorrow. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:6">59:6</a> Thou hast given a warning to them that fear thee: that they may flee from before the bow: That thy beloved may be delivered. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:7">59:7</a> Save me with thy right hand, and hear me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:8">59:8</a> God hath spoken in his holy place: I will rejoice, and I will divide Sichem; and will mete out the vale of tabernacles. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:9">59:9</a> Galaad is mine, and Manasses is mine: and Ephraim is the strength of my head. Juda is my king: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:10">59:10</a> Moab is the pot of my hope. Into Edom will I stretch out my shoe: to me the foreigners are made subject. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:11">59:11</a> Who will bring me into the strong city? who will lead me into Edom? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:12">59:12</a> Wilt not thou, O God, who hast cast us off? and wilt not thou, O God, go out with our armies? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:13">59:13</a> Give us help from trouble: for vain is the salvation of man. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:14">59:14</a> Through God we shall do mightily: and he shall bring to nothing them that afflict us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:1">60:1</a> Unto the end, in hymns, for David. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:2">60:2</a> Hear, O God, my supplication: be attentive to my prayer, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:3">60:3</a> To thee have I cried from the ends of the earth: when my heart was in anguish, thou hast exalted me on a rock. Thou hast conducted me; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:4">60:4</a> for thou hast been my hope; a tower of strength against the face of the enemy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:5">60:5</a> In thy tabernacle I shall dwell for ever: I shall be protected under the covert of thy wings. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:6">60:6</a> For thou, my God, hast heard my prayer: thou hast given an inheritance to them that fear thy name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:7">60:7</a> Thou wilt add days to the days of the king: his years even to generation and generation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:8">60:8</a> He abideth for ever in the sight of God: his mercy and truth who shall search ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:9">60:9</a> So will I sing a psalm to thy name for ever and ever: that I may pay my vows from day to day. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:1">61:1</a> Unto the end, for Idithun, a psalm of David. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:2">61:2</a> Shall not my soul be subject to God? for from him is my salvation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:3">61:3</a> For he is my God and my saviour: he is my protector, I shall be moved no more. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:4">61:4</a> How long do you rush in upon a man? you all kill, as if you were thrusting down a leaning wall, and a tottering fence. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:5">61:5</a> But they have thought to cast away my price; I ran in thirst: they blessed with their mouth, but cursed with their heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:6">61:6</a> But be thou, O my soul, subject to God: for from him is my patience. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:7">61:7</a> For he is my God and my saviour: he is my helper, I shall not be moved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:8">61:8</a> In God is my salvation and my glory: he is the God of my help, and my hope is in God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:9">61:9</a> Trust in him, all ye congregation of people: pour out your hearts before him. God is our helper for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:10">61:10</a> But vain are the sons of men, the sons of men are liars in the balances: that by vanity they may together deceive. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:11">61:11</a> Trust not in iniquity, and cover not robberies: if riches abound, set not your heart upon them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:12">61:12</a> God hath spoken once, these two things have I heard, that power belongeth to God, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:13">61:13</a> and mercy to thee, O Lord; for thou wilt render to every man according to his works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:1">62:1</a> A psalm of David when he was in the desert of Edom. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:2">62:2</a> O God, my God, to thee do I watch at break of day. For thee my soul hath thirsted; for thee my flesh, O how many ways! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:3">62:3</a> In a desert land, and where there is no way, and no water: so in the sanctuary have I come before thee, to see thy power and thy glory. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:4">62:4</a> For thy mercy is better than lives: thee my lips shall praise. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:5">62:5</a> Thus will I bless thee all my life long: and in thy name I will lift up my hands. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:6">62:6</a> Let my soul be filled as with marrow and fatness: and my mouth shall praise thee with joyful lips. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:7">62:7</a> If I have remembered thee upon my bed, I will meditate on thee in the morning: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:8">62:8</a> because thou hast been my helper. And I will rejoice under the covert of thy wings: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:9">62:9</a> my soul hath stuck close to thee: thy right hand hath received me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:10">62:10</a> But they have sought my soul in vain, they shall go into the lower parts of the earth: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:11">62:11</a> They shall be delivered into the hands of the sword, they shall be the portions of foxes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:12">62:12</a> But the king shall rejoice in God, all they shall be praised that swear by him: because the mouth is stopped of them that speak wicked things. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:1">63:1</a> Unto the end, a psalm for David. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:2">63:2</a> Hear, O God, my prayer, when I make supplication to thee : deliver my soul from the fear of the enemy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:3">63:3</a> Thou hast protected me from the assembly of the malignant; from the multitude of the workers of iniquity. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:4">63:4</a> For they have whetted their tongues like a sword; they have bent their bow a bitter thing, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:5">63:5</a> to shoot in secret the undefiled. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:6">63:6</a> They will shoot at him on a sudden, and will not fear: they are resolute in wickedness. They have talked of hiding snares; they have said: Who shall see them? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:7">63:7</a> They have searched after iniquities: they have failed in their search. Man shall come to a deep heart: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:8">63:8</a> and God shall be exalted. The arrows of children are their wounds: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:9">63:9</a> and their tongues against them are made weak. All that saw them were troubled; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:10">63:10</a> and every man was afraid. And they declared the works of God: and understood his doings. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:11">63:11</a> The just shall rejoice in the Lord, and shall hope in him: and all the upright in heart shall be praised. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:1">64:1</a> To the end, a psalm of David. The canticle of Jeremias and Ezechiel to the people of the captivity, when they began to go out. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:2">64:2</a> A Hymn, O God, becometh thee in Sion: and a vow shall be paid to thee in Jerusalem. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:3">64:3</a> O hear my prayer: all flesh shall come to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:4">64:4</a> The words of the wicked have prevailed over us: and thou wilt pardon our transgressions. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:5">64:5</a> Blessed is he whom thou hast chosen and taken to thee: he shall dwell in thy courts. We shall be filled with the good things of thy house; holy is thy temple, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:6">64:6</a> wonderful in justice. Hear us, O God our saviour, who art the hope of all the ends of the earth, and in the sea afar off. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:7">64:7</a> Thou who preparest the mountains by thy strength, being girded with power: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:8">64:8</a> who troublest the depth of the sea, the noise of its waves. The Gentiles shall be troubled, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:9">64:9</a> and they that dwell in the uttermost borders shall be afraid at thy signs: thou shalt make the outgoings of the morning and of the evening to be joyful. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:10">64:10</a> Thou hast visited the earth, and hast plentifully watered it; thou hast many ways enriched it. The river of God is filled with water, thou hast prepared their food: for so is its preparation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:11">64:11</a> Fill up plentifully the streams thereof, multiply its fruits; it shall spring up and rejoice in its showers. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:12">64:12</a> Thou shalt bless the crown of the year of thy goodness: and thy fields shall be filled with plenty. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:13">64:13</a> The beautiful places of the wilderness shall grow fat: and the hills shall be girded about with joy, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:14">64:14</a> The rams of the flock are clothed, and the vales shall abound with corn: they shall shout, yea they shall sing a hymn. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:1">65:1</a> Unto the end, a canticle of a psalm of the resurrection. Shout with joy to God, all the earth, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:2">65:2</a> sing ye a psalm to his name; give glory to his praise. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:3">65:3</a> Say unto God, How terrible are thy works, O Lord! in the multitude of thy strength thy enemies shall lie to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:4">65:4</a> Let all the earth adore thee, and sing to thee: let it sing a psalm to thy name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:5">65:5</a> Come and see the works of God; who is terrible in his counsels over the sons of men. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:6">65:6</a> Who turneth the sea into dry land, in the river they shall pass on foot: there shall we rejoice in him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:7">65:7</a> Who by his power ruleth for ever: his eyes behold the nations; let not them that provoke him he exalted in themselves. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:8">65:8</a> O bless our God, ye Gentiles: and make the voice of his praise to be heard. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:9">65:9</a> Who hath set my soul to live: and hath not suffered my feet to be moved: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:10">65:10</a> For thou, O God, hast proved us: thou hast tried us by fire, as silver is tried. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:11">65:11</a> Thou hast brought us into a net, thou hast laid afflictions on our back: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:12">65:12</a> thou hast set men over our heads. We have passed through tire and water, and thou hast brought us out into a refreshment. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:13">65:13</a> I will go into thy house with burnt offerings: I will pay thee my vows, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:14">65:14</a> which my lips have uttered, And my mouth hath spoken, when I was in trouble. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:15">65:15</a> I will offer up to thee holocausts full of marrow, with burnt offerings of rams: I will offer to thee bullocks with goats. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:16">65:16</a> Come and hear, all ye that fear God, and I will tell you what great things he hath done for my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:17">65:17</a> I cried to him with my mouth: and I extolled him with my tongue. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:18">65:18</a> If I have looked at iniquity in my heart, the Lord will not hear me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:19">65:19</a> Therefore hath God heard me, and hath attended to the voice of my supplication. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:20">65:20</a> Blessed be God, who hath not turned away my prayer, nor his mercy from me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:1">66:1</a> Unto the end, in, hymns, a psalm of a canticle for David. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:2">66:2</a> May God have mercy on us, and bless us: may he cause the light of his countenance to shine upon us, and may he have mercy on us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:3">66:3</a> That we may know thy way upon earth: thy salvation in all nations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:4">66:4</a> Let people confess to thee, O God: let all people give praise to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:5">66:5</a> Let the nations be glad and rejoice: for thou judgest the people with justice, and directest the nations upon earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:6">66:6</a> Let the people, O God, confess to thee: let all the people give praise to thee: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:7">66:7</a> the earth hath yielded her fruit. May God, our God bless us, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:8">66:8</a> may God bless us: and all the ends of the earth fear him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:1">67:1</a> Unto the end, a psalm of a canticle for David himself. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:2">67:2</a> Let God arise, and let his enemies be scattered: and let them that hate him flee from before his face. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:3">67:3</a> As smoke vanisheth, so let them vanish away: as wax melteth before the fire, so let the wicked perish at the presence of God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:4">67:4</a> And let the just feast, and rejoice before God: and be delighted with gladness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:5">67:5</a> Sing ye to God, sing a psalm to his name, make a way for him who ascendeth upon the west: the Lord is his name. Rejoice ye before him: but the wicked shall be troubled at his presence, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:6">67:6</a> who is the father of orphans, and the judge of widows. God in his holy place: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:7">67:7</a> God who maketh men of one manner to dwell in a house: Who bringeth out them that were bound in strength; in like manner them that provoke, that dwell in sepulchres. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:8">67:8</a> O God, when thou didst go forth in the sight of thy people, when thou didst pass through the desert: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:9">67:9</a> The earth was moved, and the heavens dropped at the presence of the God of Sina, at the presence of the God of Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:10">67:10</a> Thou shalt set aside for thy inheritance a free rain, O God: and it was weakened, but thou hast made it perfect. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:11">67:11</a> In it shall thy animals dwell; in thy sweetness, O God, thou hast provided for the poor. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:12">67:12</a> The Lord shall give the word to them that preach good tidings with great power. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:13">67:13</a> The king of powers is of the beloved, of the beloved; and the beauty of the house shall divide spoils. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:14">67:14</a> If you sleep among the midst of lots, you shall be as the wings of a dove covered with silver, and the hinder parts of her back with the paleness of gold. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:15">67:15</a> When he that is in heaven appointeth kings over her, they shall be whited with snow in Selmon. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:16">67:16</a> The mountain of God is a fat mountain. A curdled mountain, a fat mountain. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:17">67:17</a> Why suspect, ye curdled mountains? A mountain in which God is well pleased to dwell: for there the Lord shall dwell unto the end. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:18">67:18</a> The chariot of God is attended by ten thousands; thousands of them that rejoice: the Lord is among them in Sina, in the holy place. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:19">67:19</a> Thou hast ascended on high, thou hast led captivity captive; thou hast received gifts in men. Yea for those also that do not believe, the dwelling of the Lord God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:20">67:20</a> Blessed be the Lord day by day: the God of our salvation will make our journey prosperous to us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:21">67:21</a> Our God is the God of salvation: and of the Lord, of the Lord are the issues from death. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:22">67:22</a> But God shall break the heads of his enemies: the hairy crown of them that walk on in their sins. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:23">67:23</a> The Lord said: I will turn them from Basan, I will turn them into the depth of the sea: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:24">67:24</a> That thy foot may be dipped in the blood of thy enemies; the tongue of thy dogs be red with the same. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:25">67:25</a> They have seen thy goings, O God, the goings of my God: of my king who is in his sanctuary. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:26">67:26</a> Princes went before joined with singers, in the midst of young damsels playing on timbrels. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:27">67:27</a> In the churches bless ye God the Lord, from the fountains of Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:28">67:28</a> There is Benjamin a youth, in ecstasy of mind. The princes of Juda are their leaders: the princes of Zabulon, the princes of Nephthali. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:29">67:29</a> Command thy strength, O God: confirm, O God, what thou hast wrought in us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:30">67:30</a> From thy temple in Jerusalem, kings shall offer presents to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:31">67:31</a> Rebuke the wild beasts of the reeds, the congregation of bulls with the kine of the people; who seek to exclude them who are tried with silver. Scatter thou the nations that delight in wars: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:32">67:32</a> ambassadors shall come out of Egypt: Ethiopia shall soon stretch out her hands to God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:33">67:33</a> Sing to God, ye kingdoms of the earth: sing ye to the Lord: Sing ye to God, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:34">67:34</a> who mounteth above the heaven of heavens, to the east. Behold he will give to his voice the voice of power: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:35">67:35</a> give ye glory to God for Israel, his magnificence, and his power is in the clouds. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:36">67:36</a> God is wonderful in his saints: the God of Israel is he who will give power and strength to his people. Blessed be God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:1">68:1</a> Unto the end, for them that shall be changed; for David. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:2">68:2</a> Save me, O God: for the waters are come in even unto my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:3">68:3</a> I stick fast in the mire of the deep: and there is no sure standing. I am come into the depth of the sea: and a tempest hath overwhelmed me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:4">68:4</a> I have laboured with crying; my jaws are become hoarse: my eyes have failed, whilst I hope in my God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:5">68:5</a> They are multiplied above the hairs of my head, who hate me without cause. My enemies are grown strong who have wrongfully persecuted me: then did I pay that which I took not away. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:6">68:6</a> O God, thou knowest my foolishness; and my offences are not hidden from thee: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:7">68:7</a> Let not them be ashamed for me, who look for thee, O Lord, the Lord of hosts. Let them not be confounded on my account, who seek thee, O God of Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:8">68:8</a> Because for thy sake I have borne reproach; shame hath covered my face. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:9">68:9</a> I am become a stranger to my brethren, and an alien to the sons of my mother. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:10">68:10</a> For the zeal of thy house hath eaten me up: and the reproaches of them that reproached thee are fallen upon me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:11">68:11</a> And I covered my soul in fasting: and it was made a reproach to me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:12">68:12</a> And I made haircloth my garment: and I became a byword to them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:13">68:13</a> They that sat in the gate spoke against me: and they that drank wine made me their song. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:14">68:14</a> But as for me, my prayer is to thee, O Lord; for the time of thy good pleasure, O God. In the multitude of thy mercy hear me, in the truth of thy salvation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:15">68:15</a> Draw me out of the mire, that I may not stick fast: deliver me from them that hate me, and out of the deep waters. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:16">68:16</a> Let not the tempest of water drown me, nor the deep swallow me up: and let not the pit shut her mouth upon me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:17">68:17</a> Hear me, O Lord, for thy mercy is kind; look upon me according to the multitude of thy tender mercies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:18">68:18</a> And turn not away thy face from thy servant: for I am in trouble, hear me speedily. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:19">68:19</a> Attend to my soul, and deliver it: save me because of my enemies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:20">68:20</a> Thou knowest my reproach, and my confusion, and my shame. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:21">68:21</a> In thy sight are all they that afflict me; my heart hath expected reproach and misery. And I looked for one that would grieve together with me, but there was none: and for one that would comfort me, and I found none. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:22">68:22</a> And they gave me gall for my food, and in my thirst they gave me vinegar to drink. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:23">68:23</a> Let their table become as a snare before them, and a recompense, and a stumblingblock. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:24">68:24</a> Let their eyes be darkened that they see not; and their back bend thou down always. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:25">68:25</a> Pour out thy indignation upon them: and let thy wrathful anger take hold of them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:26">68:26</a> Let their habitation be made desolate: and let there be none to dwell in their tabernacles. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:27">68:27</a> Because they have persecuted him whom thou hast smitten; and they have added to the grief of my wounds. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:28">68:28</a> Add thou iniquity upon their iniquity: and let them not come into thy justice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:29">68:29</a> Let them be blotted out of the book of the living; and with the just let them not be written. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:30">68:30</a> But I am poor and sorrowful: thy salvation, O God, hath set me up. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:31">68:31</a> I will praise the name of God with a canticle: and I will magnify him with praise. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:32">68:32</a> And it shall please God better than a young calf, that bringeth forth horns and hoofs. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:33">68:33</a> Let the poor see and rejoice: seek ye God, and your soul shall live. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:34">68:34</a> For the Lord hath heard the poor: and hath not despised his prisoners. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:35">68:35</a> Let the heavens and the earth praise him; the sea, and every thing that creepeth therein. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:36">68:36</a> For God will save Sion, and the cities of Juda shall be built up. And they shall dwell there, and acquire it by inheritance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:37">68:37</a> And the seed of his servants shall possess it; and they that love his name shall dwell therein. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:1">69:1</a> Unto the end, a psalm for David, to bring to remembrance that the Lord saved him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:2">69:2</a> O God, come to my assistance; O Lord, make haste to help me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:3">69:3</a> Let them be confounded and ashamed that seek my soul: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:4">69:4</a> Let them be turned backward, and blush for shame that desire evils to me: Let them be presently turned away blushing for shame that say to me: 'T is well, 't is well. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:5">69:5</a> Let all that seek thee rejoice and be glad in thee; and let such as love thy salvation say always: The Lord be magnified. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:6">69:6</a> But I am needy and poor; O God, help me. Thou art my helper and my deliverer: O Lord, make no delay. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:1">70:1</a> A psalm for David. Of the sons of Jonadab, and the former captives. In thee, O Lord, I have hoped, let me never be put to confusion: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:2">70:2</a> deliver me in thy justice, and rescue me. Incline thy ear unto me, and save me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:3">70:3</a> Be thou unto me a God, a protector, and a place of strength: that thou mayst make me safe. For thou art my firmament and my refuge. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:4">70:4</a> Deliver me, O my God, out of the hand of the sinner, and out of the hand of the transgressor of the law and of the unjust. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:5">70:5</a> For thou art my patience, O Lord: my hope, O Lord, from my youth; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:6">70:6</a> By thee have I been confirmed from the womb: from my mother's womb thou art my protector. Of thee shall I continually sing: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:7">70:7</a> I run become unto many as a wonder, but thou art a strong helper. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:8">70:8</a> Let my mouth be filled with praise, that I may sing thy glory; thy greatness all the day long. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:9">70:9</a> Cast me not off in the time of old age: when my strength shall fail, do not thou forsake me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:10">70:10</a> For my enemies have spoken against me; and they that watched my soul have consulted together, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:11">70:11</a> Saying: God hath forsaken him: pursue and take him, for there is none to deliver him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:12">70:12</a> O God, be not thou far from me: O my God, make haste to my help. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:13">70:13</a> Let them be confounded and come to nothing that detract my soul; let them be covered with confusion and shame that seek my hurt. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:14">70:14</a> But I will always hope; and will add to all thy praise. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:15">70:15</a> My mouth shall shew forth thy justice; thy salvation all the day long. Because I have not knows learning, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:16">70:16</a> I will enter into the powers of the Lord: O Lord, I will be mindful of thy justice alone. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:17">70:17</a> Thou hast taught me, O God, from my youth: and till now I will declare thy wonderful works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:18">70:18</a> And unto old age and grey hairs: O God, forsake me not, Until I shew forth thy arm to all the generation that is to come: Thy power, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:19">70:19</a> and thy justice, O God, even to the highest great things thou hast done: O God, who is like to thee? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:20">70:20</a> How great troubles hast thou shewn me, many and grievous: and turning thou hast brought me to life, and hast brought me back again from the depths of the earth : </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:21">70:21</a> Thou hast multiplied thy magnificence; and turning to me thou hast comforted me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:22">70:22</a> For I will also confess to thee thy truth with the instruments of psaltery: O God, I will sing to thee with the harp, thou holy one of Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:23">70:23</a> My lips shall greatly rejoice, when I shall sing to thee; and my soul which thou hast redeemed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:24">70:24</a> Yea and my tongue shall meditate on thy justice all the day; when they shall be confounded and put to shame that seek evils to me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:1">71:1</a> A psalm on Solomon. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:2">71:2</a> Give to the king thy judgment, O God: and to the king's son thy justice: To judge thy people with justice, and thy poor with judgment. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:3">71:3</a> Let the mountains receive peace for the people: and the hills justice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:4">71:4</a> He shall judge the poor of the people, and he shall save the children of the poor: and he shall humble the oppressor. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:5">71:5</a> And he shall continue with the sun, and before the moon, throughout all generations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:6">71:6</a> He shall come down like rain upon the fleece; and as showers falling gently upon the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:7">71:7</a> In his days shall justice spring up, and abundance of peace, till the moon be taken sway. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:8">71:8</a> And he shall rule from sea to sea, and from the river unto the ends of the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:9">71:9</a> Before him the Ethiopians shall fall down: and his enemies shall lick the ground. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:10">71:10</a> The kings of Tharsis and the islands shall offer presents: the kings of the Arabians and of Saba shall bring gifts: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:11">71:11</a> And all kings of the earth shall adore him: all nations shall serve him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:12">71:12</a> For he shall deliver the poor from the mighty: and the needy that had no helper. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:13">71:13</a> He shall spare the poor and needy: and he shall save the souls of the poor. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:14">71:14</a> He shall redeem their souls from usuries and iniquity: and their names shall be honourable in his sight. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:15">71:15</a> And he shall live, and to him shall be given of the gold of Arabia, for him they shall always adore: they shall bless him all the day. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:16">71:16</a> And there shall be a firmament on the earth on the tops of mountains, above Libanus shall the fruit thereof be exalted : and they of the city shall flourish like the grass of the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:17">71:17</a> Let his name be blessed for evermore : his name continueth before the sun. And in him shall all the tribes of the earth be blessed: all nations shall magnify him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:18">71:18</a> Blessed be the Lord, the God of Israel, who alone doth wonderful things. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:19">71:19</a> And blessed be the name of his majesty for ever: and the whole earth shall be filled with his majesty. So be it. So be it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:20">71:20</a> The praises of David, the son of Jesse, are ended. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:1">72:1</a> A psalm for Asaph. How good is God to Israel, to them that are of a right heart! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:2">72:2</a> But my feet were almost moved; my steps had well nigh slipped. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:3">72:3</a> Because I had a zeal on occasion of the wicked, seeing the prosperity of sinners. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:4">72:4</a> For there is no regard to their death, nor is there strength in their stripes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:5">72:5</a> They are not in the labour of men: neither shall they be scourged like other men.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:6">72:6</a> Therefore pride hath held them fast: they are covered with their iniquity and their wickedness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:7">72:7</a> Their iniquity hath come forth, as it were from fatness: they have passed into the affection of the heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:8">72:8</a> They have thought and spoken wickedness: they have spoken iniquity on high. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:9">72:9</a> They have set their mouth against heaven: and their tongue hath passed through the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:10">72:10</a> Therefore will my people return here and full days shall be found in them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:11">72:11</a> And they said: How doth God know? and is there knowledge in the most High? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:12">72:12</a> Behold these are sinners; and yet abounding in the world they have obtained riches. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:13">72:13</a> And I said: Then have I in vain justified my heart, and washed my hands among the innocent. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:14">72:14</a> And I have been scourged all the day; and my chastisement hath been in the mornings. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:15">72:15</a> If I said: I will speak thus; behold I should condemn the generation of thy children. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:16">72:16</a> I studied that I might know this thing, it is a labour in my sight: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:17">72:17</a> Until I go into the sanctuary of God, and understand concerning their last ends. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:18">72:18</a> But indeed for deceits thou hast put it to them: when they were lifted up thou hast cast them down. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:19">72:19</a> How are they brought to desolation? they have suddenly ceased to be: they have perished by reason of their iniquity. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:20">72:20</a> As the dream of them that awake, O Lord; so in thy city thou shalt bring their image to nothing. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:21">72:21</a> For my heart hath been inflamed, and my reins have been changed: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:22">72:22</a> and I am brought to nothing, and I knew not. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:23">72:23</a> I am become as a beast before thee: and I am always with thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:24">72:24</a> Thou hast held me by my right hand; and by thy will thou hast conducted me, and with thy glory thou hast received me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:25">72:25</a> For what have I in heaven? and besides thee what do I desire upon earth? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:26">72:26</a> For thee my flesh and my heart hath fainted away: thou art the God of my heart, and the God that is my portion for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:27">72:27</a> For behold they that go far from thee shall perish: thou hast destroyed all them that are disloyal to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:28">72:28</a> But it is good for me to adhere to my God, to put my hope in the Lord God: That I may declare all thy praises, in the gates of the daughter of Sion. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:1">73:1</a> Understanding for Asaph. O God, why hast thou cast us off unto the end: why is thy wrath enkindled against the sheep of thy pasture? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:2">73:2</a> Remember thy congregation, which thou hast possessed from the beginning. The sceptre of thy inheritance which thou hast redeemed: mount Sion in which thou hast dwelt. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:3">73:3</a> Lift up thy hands against their pride unto the end; see what things the enemy hath done wickedly in the sanctuary. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:4">73:4</a> And they that hate thee have made their boasts, in the midst of thy solemnity. They have set up their ensigns for signs, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:5">73:5</a> and they knew not both in the going out and on the highest top. As with axes in a wood of trees, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:6">73:6</a> they have cut down at once the gates thereof, with axe and hatchet they have brought it down. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:7">73:7</a> They have set fire to thy sanctuary: they have defiled the dwelling place of thy name on the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:8">73:8</a> They said in their heart, the whole kindred of them together: Let us abolish all the festival days of God from the land. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:9">73:9</a> Our signs we have not seen, there is now no prophet: and he will know us no more. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:10">73:10</a> How long, O God, shall the enemy reproach: is the adversary to provoke thy name for ever? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:11">73:11</a> Why dost thou turn away thy hand: and thy right hand out of the midst of thy bosom for ever ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:12">73:12</a> But God is our king before ages: he hath wrought salvation in the midst of the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:13">73:13</a> Thou by thy strength didst make the sea firm: thou didst crush the heads of the dragons in the waters. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:14">73:14</a> Thou hast broken the heads of the dragon: thou hast given him to be meat for the people of the Ethiopians. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:15">73:15</a> Thou hast broken up the fountains and the torrents: thou hast dried up the Ethan rivers. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:16">73:16</a> Thine is the day, and thine is the night: thou hast made the morning light and the sun. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:17">73:17</a> Thou hast made all the borders of the earth: the summer and the spring were formed by thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:18">73:18</a> Remember this, the enemy hath reproached the Lord: and a foolish people hath provoked thy name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:19">73:19</a> Deliver not up to beasts the souls that confess to thee: and forget not to the end the souls of thy poor. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:20">73:20</a> Have regard to thy covenant: for they that are the obscure of the earth have been filled with dwellings of iniquity. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:21">73:21</a> Let not the humble be turned away with confusion: the poor and needy shall praise thy name. </p>
