 <p><a name="an_73:22">73:22</a> Arise, O God, judge thy own cause: remember thy reproaches with which the foolish man hath reproached thee all the day. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:23">73:23</a> Forget not the voices of thy enemies: the pride of them that hate thee ascendeth continually. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:1">74:1</a> Unto the end, corrupt not, a psalm of a canticle for Asaph. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:2">74:2</a> We will praise thee, O God: we will praise, and we will call upon thy name. We will relate thy wondrous works: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:3">74:3</a> when I shall take a time, I will judge justices. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:4">74:4</a> The earth is melted, and all that dwell therein: I have established the pillars thereof. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:5">74:5</a> I said to the wicked: Do not act wickedly: and to the sinners: Lift not up the horn. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:6">74:6</a> Lift not up your horn on high: speak not iniquity against God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:7">74:7</a> For neither from the east, nor from the west, nor from the desert hills: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:8">74:8</a> for God is the judge. One he putteth down, and another he lifteth up: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:9">74:9</a> for in the hand of the Lord there is a cup of strong wine full of mixture. And he hath poured it out from this to that: but the dregs thereof are not emptied: all the sinners of the earth shall drink. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:10">74:10</a> But I will declare for ever: I will sing to the God of Jacob. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:11">74:11</a> And I will break all the horns of sinners: but the horns of the just shall be exalted. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:1">75:1</a> Unto the end, in praises, a psalm for Asaph: a canticle to the Assyrians. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:2">75:2</a> In Judea God is known: his name is great in Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:3">75:3</a> And his place is in peace: and his abode in Sion: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:4">75:4</a> There hath he broken the powers of bows, the shield, the sword, and the battie. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:5">75:5</a> Thou enlightenest wonderfully from the everlasting hills. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:6">75:6</a> All the foolish of heart were troubled. They have slept their sleep; and all the men of riches have found nothing in their hands. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:7">75:7</a> At thy rebuke, O God of Jacob, they have all slumbered that mounted on horseback. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:8">75:8</a> Thou art terrible, and who shall resist thee? from that time thy wrath. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:9">75:9</a> Thou hast caused judgment to be heard from heaven: the earth trembled and was still, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:10">75:10</a> When God arose in judgment, to save all the meek of the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:11">75:11</a> For the thought of man shall give praise to thee: and the remainders of the thought shall keep holiday to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:12">75:12</a> Vow ye, and pay to the Lord your God: all you that are round about him bring presents. To him that is terrible, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:13">75:13</a> even to him who taketh away the spirit of princes: to the terrible with the kings of the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:1">76:1</a> Unto the end, for Idithun, a psalm of Asaph. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:2">76:2</a> I cried to the Lord with my voice; to God with my voice, and he gave ear to me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:3">76:3</a> In the day of my trouble I sought God, with my hands lifted up to him in the night, and I was not deceived. My soul refused to be comforted: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:4">76:4</a> I remembered God, and was delighted, and was exercised, and my spirit swooned away. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:5">76:5</a> My eyes prevented the watches: I was troubled, and I spoke not. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:6">76:6</a> I thought upon the days of old: and I had in my mind the eternal years. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:7">76:7</a> And I meditated in the night with my own heart: and I was exercised and I swept my spirit. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:8">76:8</a> Will God then cast off for ever? or will he never be more favourable again? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:9">76:9</a> Or will he cut off his mercy for ever, from generation to generation? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:10">76:10</a> Or will God forget to shew mercy? or will he in his anger shut up his mercies? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:11">76:11</a> And I said, Now have I begun: this is the change of the right hand of the most High. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:12">76:12</a> I remembered the works of the Lord: for I will be mindful of thy wonders from the beginning. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:13">76:13</a> And I will meditate on all thy works: and will be employed in thy inventions. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:14">76:14</a> Thy way, O God, is in the holy place: who is the great God like our God? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:15">76:15</a> Thou art the God that dost wonders. Thou hast made thy power known among the nations: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:16">76:16</a> with thy arm thou hast redeemed thy people the children of Jacob and of Joseph. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:17">76:17</a> The waters saw thee, O God, the waters saw thee: and they were afraid, and the depths were troubled. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:18">76:18</a> Great was the noise of the waters: the clouds sent out a sound. For thy arrows pass: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:19">76:19</a> the voice of thy thunder in a wheel. Thy lightnings enlightened the world: the earth shook and trembled. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:20">76:20</a> Thy way is in the sea, and thy paths in many waters: and thy footsteps shall not be known. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:21">76:21</a> Thou hast conducted thy people like sheep, by the hand of Moses and Aaron </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:1">77:1</a> Understanding for Asaph. Attend, O my people, to my law: incline your ears to the words of my mouth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:2">77:2</a> I will open my mouth in parables: I will utter propositions from the beginning. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:3">77:3</a> How great things have we heard and known, and our fathers have told us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:4">77:4</a> They have not been hidden from their children, in another generation. Declaring the praises of the Lord, and his powers, and his wonders which he hath done. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:5">77:5</a> And he set up a testimony in Jacob: and made a law in Israel. How great things he commanded our fathers, that they should make the same known to their children: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:6">77:6</a> that another generation might know them. The children that should be born and should rise up, and declare them to their children. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:7">77:7</a> That they may put their hope in God and may not forget the works of God: and may seek his commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:8">77:8</a> That they may not become like their fathers, a perverse end exasperating generation. A generation that set not their heart aright: and whose spirit was not faithful to God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:9">77:9</a> The sons of Ephraim who bend and shoot with the bow: they have turned back in the day of battle. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:10">77:10</a> They kept not the covenant of God: and in his law they would not walk. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:11">77:11</a> And they forgot his benefits, and his wonders that he had shewn them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:12">77:12</a> Wonderful things did he do in the sight of their fathers, in the land of Egypt, in the field of Tanis. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:13">77:13</a> He divided the sea and brought them through: and he made the waters to stand as in a vessel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:14">77:14</a> And he conducted them with a cloud by day: and all the night with a light of </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:15">77:15</a> He struck the rock in the wilderness: and gave them to drink, as out of the great deep. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:16">77:16</a> He brought forth water out of the rock: and made streams run down as rivers. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:17">77:17</a> And they added yet more sin against him: they provoked the most High to wrath in the place without water. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:18">77:18</a> And they tempted God in their hearts, by asking meat for their desires. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:19">77:19</a> And they spoke ill of God: they said: Can God furnish a table in the wilderness? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:20">77:20</a> Because he struck the rock, and the waters gushed out, and the streams overflowed. Can he also give bread, or provide a table for his people? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:21">77:21</a> Therefore the Lord heard, and was angry: and a fire was kindled against Jacob, and wrath came up against Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:22">77:22</a> Because they believed not in God: and trusted not in his salvation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:23">77:23</a> And he had commanded the clouds from above, and had opened the doors of heaven. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:24">77:24</a> And had rained down manna upon them to eat, and had given them the bread of heaven. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:25">77:25</a> Man ate the bread of angels: he sent them provisions in abundance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:26">77:26</a> He removed the south wind from heaven: and by his power brought in the southwest wind. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:27">77:27</a> And he rained upon them flesh as dust: and feathered fowls like as the sand of the sea. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:28">77:28</a> And they fell in the midst of their camp, round about their pavilions. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:29">77:29</a> So they did eat, and were filled exceedingly, and he gave them their desire: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:30">77:30</a> they were not defrauded of that which they craved. As yet their meat was in their mouth: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:31">77:31</a> and the wrath of God came upon them. And he slew the fat ones amongst them, and brought down the chosen men of Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:32">77:32</a> In all these things they sinned still: and they believed not for his wondrous works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:33">77:33</a> And their days were consumed in vanity, and their years in haste. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:34">77:34</a> When he slew them, then they sought him: and they returned, and came to him early in the morning. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:35">77:35</a> And they remembered that God was their helper: and the most high God their redeemer. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:36">77:36</a> And they loved him with their mouth: and with their tongue they lied unto him: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:37">77:37</a> But their heart was not right with him: nor were they counted faithful in his covenant. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:38">77:38</a> But he is merciful, and will forgive their sins: and will not destroy them. And many a time did he turn away his anger: and did not kindle all his wrath. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:39">77:39</a> And he remembered that they are flesh: a wind that goeth and returneth not. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:40">77:40</a> How often did they provoke him in the desert: and move him to wrath in the place without water? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:41">77:41</a> And they turned back and tempted God: and grieved the holy one of Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:42">77:42</a> They remembered not his hand, in the day that he redeemed them from the hand of him that afflicted them: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:43">77:43</a> How he wrought his signs in Egypt, and his wonders in the field of Tanis. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:44">77:44</a> And he turned their rivers into blood, and their showers that they might, not drink. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:45">77:45</a> He sent amongst them divers sores of flies, which devoured them: and frogs which destroyed them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:46">77:46</a> And he gave up their fruits to the blast, and their labours to the locust. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:47">77:47</a> And he destroyed their vineyards with hail, and their mulberry trees with hoarfrost. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:48">77:48</a> And he gave up their cattle to the hail, and their stock to the fire. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:49">77:49</a> And he sent upon them the wrath of his indignation: indignation and wrath and trouble, which he sent by evil angels. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:50">77:50</a> He made a way for a path to his anger: he spared not their souls from death, and their cattle he shut up in death. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:51">77:51</a> And he killed all the firstborn in the land of Egypt: the firstfruits of all their labour in the tabernacles of Cham. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:52">77:52</a> And he took away his own people as sheep: and guided them in the wilderness like a flock. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:53">77:53</a> And he brought them out in hope, and they feared not: and the sea overwhelmed their enemies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:54">77:54</a> And he brought them into the mountain of his sanctuary: the mountain which his right hand had purchased. And he cast out the Gentiles before them: and by lot divided to them their land by a line of distribution. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:55">77:55</a> And he made the tribes of Israel to dwell in their tabernacles. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:56">77:56</a> Yet they tempted, and provoked the most high God: and they kept not his testimonies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:57">77:57</a> And they turned away, and kept not the covenant: even like their fathers they were turned aside as a crooked bow. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:58">77:58</a> They provoked him to anger on their hills: and moved him to jealousy with their graven things. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:59">77:59</a> God heard, and despised them, and he reduced Israel exceedingly as it were to nothing. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:60">77:60</a> And he put away the tabernacle of Silo, his tabernacle where he dwelt among men. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:61">77:61</a> And he delivered their strength into captivity: and their beauty into the hands of the enemy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:62">77:62</a> And he shut up his people under the sword: and he despised his inheritance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:63">77:63</a> Fire consumed their young men: and their maidens were not lamented. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:64">77:64</a> Their priests fell by the sword: and their widows did not mourn. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:65">77:65</a> And the Lord was awaked as one out of sleep, and like a mighty man that hath been surfeited with wine. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:66">77:66</a> And he smote his enemies on the hinder parts: he put them to an everlasting reproach. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:67">77:67</a> And he rejected the tabernacle of Joseph: and chose not the tribe of Ephraim: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:68">77:68</a> But he chose the tribe of Juda, mount Sion which he loved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:69">77:69</a> And he built his sanctuary as of unicorns, in the land which he founded for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:70">77:70</a> And he chose his servant David, and took him from the hocks of sheep: he brought him from following the ewes great with young, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:71">77:71</a> To feed Jacob his servant, and Israel his inheritance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:72">77:72</a> And he fed them in the innocence of his heart: and conducted them by the skilfulness of his hands. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:1">78:1</a> A psalm for Asaph. O God, the heathens are come into thy inheritance, they have defiled thy holy temple: they have made Jerusalem as a place to keep fruit. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:2">78:2</a> They have given the dead bodies of thy servants to be meat for the fowls of the air: the flesh of thy saints for the beasts of the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:3">78:3</a> They have poured out their blood as water, round about Jerusalem and there was none to bury them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:4">78:4</a> We are become a reproach to our neighbours: a scorn and derision to them that are round about us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:5">78:5</a> How long, O Lord, wilt thou be angry for ever: shall thy zeal be kindled like a fire? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:6">78:6</a> Pour out thy wrath upon the nations that have not known thee: and upon the kingdoms that have not called upon thy name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:7">78:7</a> Because they have devoured Jacob; and have laid waste his place. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:8">78:8</a> Remember not our former iniquities: let thy mercies speedily prevent us, for we are become exceeding poor. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:9">78:9</a> Help us, O God, our saviour: and for the glory of thy name, O Lord, deliver us: and forgive us our sins for thy name's sake: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:10">78:10</a> Lest they should say among the Gentiles: Where is their God? And let him be made known among the nations before our eyes, By the revenging the blood of thy servants, which hath been shed: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:11">78:11</a> let the sighing of the prisoners come in before thee. According to the greatness of thy arm, take possession of the children of them that have been put to death. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:12">78:12</a> And render to our neighbours sevenfold in their bosom: the reproach wherewith they have reproached thee, O Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:13">78:13</a> But we thy people, and the sheep of thy pasture, will give thanks to thee for ever. We will shew forth thy praise, unto generation and generation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:1">79:1</a> Unto the end, for them that shall he changed, a testimony for Asaph, a psalm. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:2">79:2</a> Give ear, O thou that rulest Israel: thou that leadest Joseph like a sheep. Thou that sittest upon the cherubims, shine forth </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:3">79:3</a> before Ephraim, Benjamin, and Manasses. Stir up thy might, and come to save us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:4">79:4</a> Convert us, O God: and shew us thy face, and we shall be saved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:5">79:5</a> O Lord God of hosts, how long wilt thou be angry against the prayer of thy servant? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:6">79:6</a> How long wilt thou feed us with the bread of tears: and give us for our drink tears in measure? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:7">79:7</a> Thou hast made us to be a contradiction to our neighbours: and our enemies have scoffed at us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:8">79:8</a> O God of hosts, convert us: and shew thy face, and we shall be saved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:9">79:9</a> Thou hast brought a vineyard out of Egypt: thou hast cast cut the Gentiles and planted it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:10">79:10</a> Thou wast the guide of its journey in its sight: thou plantedst the roots thereof, and it filled the land. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:11">79:11</a> The shadow of it covered the hills: and the branches thereof the cedars of God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:12">79:12</a> It stretched forth its branches unto the sea, and its boughs unto the river. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:13">79:13</a> Why hast thou broken down the hedge thereof, so that all they who pass by the way do pluck it? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:14">79:14</a> The boar out of the wood hath laid it waste: and a singular wild beast hath devoured it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:15">79:15</a> Turn again, O God of hosts, look down from heaven, and see, and visit this vineyard: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:16">79:16</a> And perfect the same which thy right hand hath planted: and upon the son of man whom thou hast confirmed for thyself. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:17">79:17</a> Things set on fire and dug down shall perish at the rebuke of thy countenance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:18">79:18</a> Let thy hand be upon the man of thy right hand: and upon the son of man whom thou hast confirmed for thyself. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:19">79:19</a> And we depart not from thee, thou shalt quicken us: and we will call upon thy name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:20">79:20</a> O Lord God of hosts, convert us: and shew thy face, and we shall be saved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:1">80:1</a> Unto the end, for the winepresses, a psalm for Asaph himself. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:2">80:2</a> Rejoice to God our helper: sing aloud to the God of Jacob. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:3">80:3</a> Take a psalm, and bring hither the timbrel: the pleasant psaltery with the harp. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:4">80:4</a> Blow up the trumpet on the new moon, on the noted day of your solemnity. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:5">80:5</a> For it is a commandment in Israel, and a judgment to the God of Jacob. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:6">80:6</a> He ordained it for a testimony in Joseph, when he came out of the land of Egypt: he heard a tongue which he knew not. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:7">80:7</a> He removed his back from the burdens: his hands had served in baskets. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:8">80:8</a> Thou calledst upon me in affliction, and I delivered thee: I heard thee in the secret place of tempest: I proved thee at the waters of contradiction. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:9">80:9</a> Hear, O my people, and I will testify to thee: O Israel, if thou wilt hearken to me, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:10">80:10</a> there shall be no new god in thee: neither shalt thou adore a strange god. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:11">80:11</a> For I am the Lord thy God, who brought thee out of the land of Egypt: open thy mouth wide, and I will fill it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:12">80:12</a> But my people heard not my voice: and Israel hearkened not to me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:13">80:13</a> So I let them go according to the desires of their heart: they shall walk in their own inventions. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:14">80:14</a> If my people had heard me: if Israel had walked in my ways: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:15">80:15</a> I should soon have humbled their enemies, and laid my hand on them that troubled them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:16">80:16</a> The enemies of the Lord have lied to him: and their time shall be for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:17">80:17</a> And he fed them with the fat of wheat, and filled them with honey out of the rock. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:1">81:1</a> A psalm for Asaph. God hath stood in the congregation of gods: and being in the midst of them he judgeth gods. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:2">81:2</a> How long will you judge unjustly: and accept the persons of the wicked? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:3">81:3</a> Judge for the needy and fatherless: do justice to the humble and the poor. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:4">81:4</a> Rescue the poor; and deliver the needy out of the hand of the sinner. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:5">81:5</a> They have not known nor understood: they walk on in darkness: all the foundations of the earth shall be moved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:6">81:6</a> I have said: You are gods and all of you the sons of the most High. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:7">81:7</a> But you like men shall die: and shall fall like one of the princes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:8">81:8</a> Arise, O God, judge thou the earth: for thou shalt inherit among all the nations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:1">82:1</a> A canticle of a psalm for Asaph. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:2">82:2</a> O God, who shall be like to thee? hold not thy peace, neither be thou still, O God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:3">82:3</a> For lo, thy enemies have made a noise: and they that hate thee have lifted up the head. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:4">82:4</a> They have taken a malicious counsel against thy people, and have consulted against thy saints. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:5">82:5</a> They have said: Come and let us destroy them, so that they be not a nation: and let the name of Israel be remembered no more. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:6">82:6</a> For they have contrived with one consent: they have made a covenant together against thee, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:7">82:7</a> the tabernacles of the Edomites, and the Ismahelites: Moab, and the Agarens, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:8">82:8</a> Gebal, and Ammon and Amalec: the Philistines, with the inhabitants of Tyre. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:9">82:9</a> Yea, and the Assyrian also is joined with them: they are come to the aid of the sons of Lot. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:10">82:10</a> Do to them as thou didst to Madian and to Sisara: as to Jabin at the brook of Cisson. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:11">82:11</a> Who perished at Endor: and became as dung for the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:12">82:12</a> Make their princes like Oreb, and Zeb, and Zebee, and Salmana. All their princes, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:13">82:13</a> who have said: Let us possess the sanctuary of God for an inheritance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:14">82:14</a> O my God, make them like a wheel; and as stubble before the wind. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:15">82:15</a> As fire which burneth the wood: and as a flame burning mountains: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:16">82:16</a> So shalt thou pursue them with thy tempest: and shalt trouble them in thy wrath. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:17">82:17</a> Fill their faces with shame; and they shall seek thy name, O Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:18">82:18</a> Let them be ashamed and troubled for ever and ever: and let them be confounded and perish. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:19">82:19</a> And let them know that the Lord is thy name: thou alone art the most High over all the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:1">83:1</a> Unto the end, for the winepresses, a psalm for the sons of Core. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:2">83:2</a> How lovely are thy tabernacles, O Lord of host! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:3">83:3</a> my soul longeth and fainteth for the courts of the Lord. My heart and my flesh have rejoiced in the living God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:4">83:4</a> For the sparrow hath found herself a house, and the turtle a nest for herself where she may lay her young ones: Thy altars, O Lord of hosts, my king and my God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:5">83:5</a> Blessed are they that dwell in thy house, O Lord: they shall praise thee for ever and ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:6">83:6</a> Blessed is the man whose help is from thee: in his heart he hath disposed to ascend by steps, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:7">83:7</a> in the vale of tears, in the place which be hath set. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:8">83:8</a> For the lawgiver shall give a blessing, they shall go from virtue to virtue: the God of gods shall be seen in Sion. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:9">83:9</a> O Lord God of hosts, hear my prayer: give ear, O God of Jacob. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:10">83:10</a> Behold, O God our protector: and look on the face of thy Christ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:11">83:11</a> For better is one day in thy courts above thousands. I have chosen to be an abject in the house of my God, rather than to dwell in the tabernacles of sinners. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:12">83:12</a> For God loveth mercy and truth: the Lord will give grace and glory. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:13">83:13</a> He will not deprive of good things them that walk in innocence : O Lord of hosts, blessed is the man that trusteth in thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:1">84:1</a> Unto the end, for the sons of Core, a psalm. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:2">84:2</a> Lord, thou hast blessed thy land: thou hast turned away the captivity of Jacob. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:3">84:3</a> Thou hast forgiven the iniquity of thy people: thou hast covered all their sins. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:4">84:4</a> Thou hast mitigated all thy anger: thou best turned away from the wrath of thy indignation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:5">84:5</a> Convert us, O God our saviour: and turn off thy anger from us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:6">84:6</a> Wilt thou be angry with us for ever: or wilt thou extend thy wrath from generation to generation? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:7">84:7</a> Thou wilt turn, O God, and bring us to life: and thy people shall rejoice in thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:8">84:8</a> Shew us, O Lord, thy mercy; and grant us thy salvation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:9">84:9</a> I will hear what the Lord God will speak in me: for he will speak peace unto his people: And unto his saints: and unto them that are converted to the heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:10">84:10</a> Surely his salvation is near to them that fear him: that glory may dwell in our land. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:11">84:11</a> Mercy and truth have met each other: justice and peace have kissed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:12">84:12</a> Truth is sprung out of the earth: and justice hath looked down from heaven. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:13">84:13</a> For the Lord will give goodness: and our earth shall yield her fruit. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:14">84:14</a> Justice shall walk before him: and shall set his steps in the way. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:1">85:1</a> A prayer for David himself. Incline thy ear, O Lord, and hear me: for I am needy and poor. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:2">85:2</a> Preserve my soul, for I am holy: save thy servant, O my God, that trusteth in thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:3">85:3</a> Have mercy on me, O Lord, for I have cried to thee all the day. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:4">85:4</a> Give joy to the soul of thy servant, for to thee, O Lord, I have lifted up my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:5">85:5</a> For thou, O Lord, art sweet and mild: and plenteous in mercy to all that call upon thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:6">85:6</a> Give ear, O Lord, to my prayer: and attend to the voice of my petition. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:7">85:7</a> I have called upon thee in the day of my trouble: because thou hast heard me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:8">85:8</a> There is none among the gods like unto thee, O Lord: and there is none according to thy works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:9">85:9</a> All the nations thou hast made shall come and adore before thee, O Lord: and they shall glorify thy name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:10">85:10</a> For thou art great and dost wonderful things: thou art God alone. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:11">85:11</a> Conduct me, O Lord, in thy way, and I will walk in thy truth: let my heart rejoice that it may fear thy name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:12">85:12</a> I will praise thee, O Lord my God: with my whole heart, and I will glorify thy name for ever: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:13">85:13</a> For thy mercy is great towards me: and thou hast delivered my soul out of the lower hell. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:14">85:14</a> O God, the wicked are risen up against me, and the assembly of the mighty have sought my soul: and they have not set thee before their eyes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:15">85:15</a> And thou, O Lord, art a God of compassion, and merciful, patient, and of much mercy, and true. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:16">85:16</a> O look upon me, and have mercy on me: give thy command to thy servant, and save the son of thy handmaid. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:17">85:17</a> Shew me a token for good: that they who hate me may see, and be confounded, because thou, O Lord, hast helped me and hast comforted me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:1">86:1</a> For the sons of Core, a psalm of a canticle. The foundations thereof are in the holy mountains: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:2">86:2</a> The Lord loveth the gates of Sion above all the tabernacles of Jacob. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:3">86:3</a> Glorious things are said of thee, O city of God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:4">86:4</a> I will be mindful of Rahab and of Babylon knowing me. Behold the foreigners, and Tyre, and the people of the Ethiopians, these were there. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:5">86:5</a> Shall not Sion say: This man and that man is born in her? and the Highest himself hath founded her. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:6">86:6</a> The Lord shall tell in his writings of peoples and of princes, of them that have been in her. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:7">86:7</a> The dwelling in thee is as it were of all rejoicing. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:1">87:1</a> A canticle of a psalm for the sons of Core: unto the end, for Maheleth, to answer understanding of Eman the Ezrahite. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:2">87:2</a> O Lord, the God of my salvation: I have cried in the day, and in the night before thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:3">87:3</a> Let my prayer come in before thee: incline thy ear to my petition. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:4">87:4</a> For my soul is filled with evils: and my life hath drawn nigh to hell. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:5">87:5</a> I am counted among them that go down to the pit: I am become as a man without help, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:6">87:6</a> free among the dead. Like the slain sleeping in the sepulchres, whom thou rememberest no more: and they are cast off from thy hand. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:7">87:7</a> They have laid me in the lower pit: in the dark places, and in the shadow of death. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:8">87:8</a> Thy wrath is strong over me: and all thy waves thou hast brought in upon me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:9">87:9</a> Thou hast put away my acquaintance far from me: they have set me an abomination to themselves. I was delivered up, and came not forth: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:10">87:10</a> my eyes languished through poverty. All the day I cried to thee, O Lord: I stretched out my hands to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:11">87:11</a> Wilt thou shew wonders to the dead? or shall physicians raise to life, and give praise to thee? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:12">87:12</a> Shall any one in the sepulchre declare thy mercy: and thy truth in destruction? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:13">87:13</a> Shall thy wonders be known in the dark; and thy justice in the land of forgetfulness? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:14">87:14</a> But I, O Lord, have cried to thee: and in the morning my prayer shall prevent thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:15">87:15</a> Lord, why castest thou off my prayer: why turnest thou away thy face from me? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:16">87:16</a> I am poor, and in labours from my youth: and being exalted have been humbled and troubled. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:17">87:17</a> Thy wrath hath come upon me: and thy terrors have troubled me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:18">87:18</a> They have come round about me like water all the day: they have compassed me about together. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:19">87:19</a> Friend and neighbour thou hast put far from me: and my acquaintance, because of misery. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:1">88:1</a> Of understanding, for Ethan the Ezrahite. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:2">88:2</a> The mercies of the Lord I will sing for ever. I will shew forth thy truth with my mouth to generation and generation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:3">88:3</a> For thou hast said: Mercy shall be built up for ever in the heavens: thy truth shall be prepared in them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:4">88:4</a> I have made a covenant with my elect: I have sworn to David my servant: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:5">88:5</a> Thy seed will I settle for ever. And I will build up thy throne unto generation and generation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:6">88:6</a> The heavens shall confess thy wonders, O Lord: and thy truth in the church of the saints. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:7">88:7</a> For who in the clouds can be compared to the Lord: or who among the sons of God shall be like to God? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:8">88:8</a> God, who is glorified in the assembly of the saints: great and terrible above all them that are about him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:9">88:9</a> O Lord God of hosts, who is like to thee? thou art mighty, O Lord, and thy truth is round about thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:10">88:10</a> Thou rulest the power of the sea: and appeasest the motion of the waves thereof. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:11">88:11</a> Thou hast humbled the proud one, as one that is slain: with the arm of thy strength thou hast scattered thy enemies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:12">88:12</a> Thine are the heavens, and thine is the earth: the world and the fulness thereof thou hast founded: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:13">88:13</a> the north and the sea thou hast created. Thabor and Hermon shall rejoice in thy name: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:14">88:14</a> thy arm is with might. Let thy hand be strengthened, and thy right hand exalted: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:15">88:15</a> justice and judgment are the preparation of thy throne. Mercy and truth shall go before thy face: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:16">88:16</a> blessed is the people that knoweth jubilation. They shall walk, O Lord, in the light of thy countenance: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:17">88:17</a> and in thy name they shall rejoice all the day, and in thy justice they shall be exalted. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:18">88:18</a> For thou art the glory of their strength: and in thy good pleasure shall our horn be exalted. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:19">88:19</a> For our protection is of the Lord, and of our king the holy one of Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:20">88:20</a> Then thou spokest in a vision to thy saints, and saidst: I have laid help upon one that is mighty, and have exalted one chosen out of my people. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:21">88:21</a> I have found David my servant: with my holy oil I have anointed him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:22">88:22</a> For my hand shall help him: and my arm shall strengthen him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:23">88:23</a> The enemy shall have no advantage over him: nor the son of iniquity have power to hurt him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:24">88:24</a> And I will cut down his enemies before his face; and them that hate him I will put to flight. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:25">88:25</a> And my truth and my mercy shall be with him: and in my name shall his horn be exalted. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:26">88:26</a> And I will set his hand in the sea; and his right hand in the rivers. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:27">88:27</a> He shall cry out to me: Thou art my father: my God, and the support of my salvation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:28">88:28</a> And I will make him my firstborn, high above the kings of the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:29">88:29</a> I will keep my mercy for him for ever: and my covenant faithful to him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:30">88:30</a> And I will make his seed to endure for evermore: and his throne as the days of heaven. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:31">88:31</a> And if his children forsake my law, and walk not in my judgments: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:32">88:32</a> If they profane my justices: and keep not my commandments: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:33">88:33</a> I will visit their iniquities with a rod: and their sins with stripes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:34">88:34</a> But my mercy I will not take away from him: nor will I suffer my truth to fail. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:35">88:35</a> Neither will I profane my covenant: and the words that proceed from my mouth I will not make void. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:36">88:36</a> Once have I sworn by my holiness: I will not lie unto David: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:37">88:37</a> his seed shall endure for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:38">88:38</a> And his throne as the sun before me: and as the moon perfect for ever, and a faithful witness in heaven. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:39">88:39</a> But thou hast rejected and despised: thou hast been angry with thy anointed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:40">88:40</a> Thou hast overthrown the covenant of thy servant: thou hast profaned his sanctuary on the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:41">88:41</a> Thou hast broken down all his hedges: thou hast made his strength fear. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:42">88:42</a> All that pass by the way have robbed him: he is become a reproach to his neighbours. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:43">88:43</a> Thou hast set up the right hand of them that oppress him: thou hast made all his enemies to rejoice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:44">88:44</a> Thou hast turned away the help of his sword; and hast not assisted him in battle. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:45">88:45</a> Thou hast made his purification to cease: and thou hast cast his throne down to the ground. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:46">88:46</a> Thou hast shortened the days of his time: thou hast covered him with confusion. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:47">88:47</a> How long, O Lord, turnest thou away unto the end? shall thy anger burn like fire? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:48">88:48</a> Remember what my substance is for hast thou made all the children of men in vain? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:49">88:49</a> Who is the man that shall live, and not see death: that shall deliver his soul from the hand of hell? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:50">88:50</a> Lord, where are thy ancient mercies, according to what thou didst swear to David in thy truth? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:51">88:51</a> Be mindful, O Lord, of the reproach of thy servants (which I have held in my bosom) of many nations: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:52">88:52</a> Wherewith thy enemies have reproached, O Lord; wherewith they have reproached the change of thy anointed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:53">88:53</a> Blessed be the Lord for evermore. So be it. So be it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:1">89:1</a> A prayer of Moses the man of God. Lord, thou hast been our refuge from generation to generation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:2">89:2</a> Before the mountains were made, or the earth and the world was formed; from eternity and to eternity thou art God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:3">89:3</a> Turn not man away to be brought low: and thou hast said: Be converted, O ye sons of men. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:4">89:4</a> For a thousand years in thy sight are as yesterday, which is past. And as a watch in the night, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:5">89:5</a> things that are counted nothing, shall their years be. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:6">89:6</a> In the morning man shall grow up like grass; in the morning he shall flourish and pass away: in the evening he shall fall, grow dry, and wither. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:7">89:7</a> For in thy wrath we have fainted away: and are troubled in thy indignation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:8">89:8</a> Thou hast set our iniquities before thy eyes: our life in the light of thy countenance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:9">89:9</a> For all our days are spent; and in thy wrath we have fainted away. Our years shall be considered spider: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:10">89:10</a> the days of our years in them are threescore and ten years. But if in the strong they be fourscore years: and what is more of them is labour and sorrow. For mildness is come upon us: and we shall be corrected. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:11">89:11</a> Who knoweth the power of thy anger, and for thy fear </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:12">89:12</a> can number thy wrath? So make thy right hand known: and men learned in heart, in wisdom. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:13">89:13</a> Return, O Lord, how long? and be entreated in favour of thy servants. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:14">89:14</a> We are filled in the morning with thy mercy: and we have rejoiced, and are delighted all our days. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:15">89:15</a> We have rejoiced for the days in which thou hast humbled us: for the years in which we have seen evils. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:16">89:16</a> Look upon thy servants and upon their works: and direct their children. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:17">89:17</a> And let the brightness of the Lord our God be upon us: and direct thou the works of our hands over us; yea, the work of our hands do thou direct. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:1">90:1</a> The praise of a canticle for David. He that dwelleth in the aid of the most High, shall abide under the protection of the God of Jacob. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:2">90:2</a> He shall say to the Lord: Thou art my protector, and my refuge: my God, in him will I trust. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:3">90:3</a> For he hath delivered me from the snare of the hunters: and from the sharp word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:4">90:4</a> He will overshadow thee with his shoulders: and under his wings thou shalt trust. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:5">90:5</a> His truth shall compass thee with a shield: thou shalt not be afraid of the terror of the night. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:6">90:6</a> Of the arrow that flieth in the day, of the business that walketh about in the dark: of invasion, or of the noonday devil. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:7">90:7</a> A thousand shall fall at thy side, and ten thousand at thy right hand: but it shall not come nigh thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:8">90:8</a> But thou shalt consider with thy eyes: and shalt see the reward of the wicked. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:9">90:9</a> Because thou, O Lord, art my hope: thou hast made the most High thy refuge. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:10">90:10</a> There shall no evil come to thee: nor shall the scourge come near thy dwelling. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:11">90:11</a> For he hath given his angels charge over thee; to keep thee in all thy ways. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:12">90:12</a> In their hands they shall bear thee up: lest thou dash thy foot against a stone. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:13">90:13</a> Thou shalt walk upon the asp and the basilisk: and thou shalt trample under foot the lion and the dragon. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:14">90:14</a> Because he hoped in me I will deliver him: I will protect him because he hath known my name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:15">90:15</a> He shall cry to me, and I will hear him: I am with him in tribulation, I will deliver him, and I will glorify him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:16">90:16</a> I will fill him with length of days; and I will shew him my salvation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:1">91:1</a> A psalm of a canticle on the sabbath day. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:2">91:2</a> It is good to give praise to the Lord: and to sing to thy name, O most High. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:3">91:3</a> To shew forth thy mercy in the morning, and thy truth in the night: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:4">91:4</a> Upon an instrument of ten strings, upon the psaltery: with a canticle upon the harp. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:5">91:5</a> For thou hast given me, O Lord, a delight in thy doings: and in the works of thy hands I shall rejoice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:6">91:6</a> O Lord, how great are thy works! thy thoughts are exceeding deep. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:7">91:7</a> The senseless man shall not know: nor will the fool understand these things. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:8">91:8</a> When the wicked shall spring up as grass: and all the workers of iniquity shall appear: That they may perish for ever and ever: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:9">91:9</a> but thou, O Lord, art most high for evermore. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:10">91:10</a> For behold thy enemies, O Lord, for behold thy enemies shall perish: and all the workers of iniquity shall be scattered. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:11">91:11</a> But my horn shall be exalted like that of the unicorn: and my old age in plentiful mercy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:12">91:12</a> My eye also hath looked down upon my enemies: and my ear shall hear of the downfall of the malignant that rise up against me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:13">91:13</a> The just shall flourish like the palm tree: he shall grow up like the cedar of Libanus. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:14">91:14</a> They that are planted in the house of the Lord shall flourish in the courts of the house of our God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:15">91:15</a> They shall still increase in a fruitful old age: and shall be well treated, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:16">91:16</a> that they may shew, That the Lord our God is righteous, and there is no iniquity in him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:1">92:1</a> The Lord hath reigned, he is clothed with beauty: the Lord is clothed with strength, and hath girded himself. For he hath established the world which shall not be moved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:2">92:2</a> Thy throne is prepared from of old: thou art from everlasting. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:3">92:3</a> The floods have lifted up, O Lord: the floods have lifted up their voice. The floods have lifted up their waves, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:4">92:4</a> with the noise of many waters. Wonderful are the surges of the sea: wonderful is the Lord on high. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:5">92:5</a> Thy testimonies are become exceedingly credible: holiness becometh thy house, O Lord, unto length of days. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:1">93:1</a> The Lord is the God to whom revenge belongeth: the God of revenge hath acted freely. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:2">93:2</a> Lift up thyself, thou that judgest the earth: render a reward to the proud. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:3">93:3</a> How long shall sinners, O Lord: how long shall sinners glory? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:4">93:4</a> Shall they utter, and speak iniquity: shall all speak who work injustice? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:5">93:5</a> Thy people, O Lord, they have brought low: and they have afflicted thy inheritance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:6">93:6</a> They have slain the widow and the stranger: and they have murdered the fatherless. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:7">93:7</a> And they have said: The Lord shall not see: neither shall the God of Jacob understand. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:8">93:8</a> Understand, ye senseless among the people: and, you fools, be wise at last. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:9">93:9</a> He that planted the ear, shall he not hear? or he that formed the eye, doth he not consider? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:10">93:10</a> He that chastiseth nations, shall he not rebuke: he that teacheth man knowledge? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:11">93:11</a> The Lord knoweth the thoughts of men, that they are vain. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:12">93:12</a> Blessed is the man whom thou shalt instruct, O Lord: and shalt teach him out of thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:13">93:13</a> That thou mayst give him rest from the evil days: till a pit be dug for the wicked. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:14">93:14</a> For the Lord will not cast off his people: neither will he forsake his own inheritance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:15">93:15</a> Until justice be turned into judgment: and they that are near it are all the upright in heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:16">93:16</a> Who shall rise up for me against the evildoers? or who shall stand with me against the workers of iniquity? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:17">93:17</a> Unless the Lord had been my helper, my soul had almost dwelt in hell. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:18">93:18</a> If I said: My foot is moved: thy mercy, O Lord, assisted me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:19">93:19</a> According to the multitude of my sorrows in my heart, thy comforts have given joy to my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:20">93:20</a> Doth the seat of iniquity stick to thee, who framest labour in commandment? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:21">93:21</a> They will hunt after the soul of the just, and will condemn innocent blood. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:22">93:22</a> But the Lord is my refuge: and my God the help of my hope. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:23">93:23</a> And he will render them their iniquity: and in their malice he will destroy them: the Lord our God will destroy them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:1">94:1</a> Come let us praise the Lord with joy: let us joyfully sing to God our saviour. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:2">94:2</a> Let us come before his presence with thanksgiving; and make a joyful noise to him with psalms. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:3">94:3</a> For the Lord is a great God, and a great King above all gods. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:4">94:4</a> For in his hand are all the ends of the earth: and the heights of the mountains are his. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:5">94:5</a> For the sea is his, and he made it: and his hands formed the dry land. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:6">94:6</a> Come let us adore and fall down: and weep before the Lord that made us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:7">94:7</a> For he is the Lord our God: and we are the people of his pasture and the sheep of his hand. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:8">94:8</a> To day if you shall hear his voice, harden not your hearts: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:9">94:9</a> As in the provocation, according to the day of temptation in the wilderness: where your fathers tempted me, they proved me, and saw my works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:10">94:10</a> Forty years long was I offended with that generation, and I said: These always err in heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:11">94:11</a> And these men have not known my ways: so I swore in my wrath that they shall not enter into my rest. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:1">95:1</a> A canticle for David himself, when the house was built after the captivity. Sing ye to the Lord a new canticle: sing to the Lord, all the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:2">95:2</a> Sing ye to the Lord and bless his name: shew forth his salvation from day to day. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:3">95:3</a> Declare his glory among the Gentiles: his wonders among all people. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:4">95:4</a> For the Lord is great, and exceedingly to be praised: he is to be feared above all gods. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:5">95:5</a> For all the gods of the Gentiles are devils: but the Lord made the heavens. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:6">95:6</a> Praise and beauty are before him: holiness and majesty in his sanctuary. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:7">95:7</a> Bring ye to the Lord, O ye kindreds of the Gentiles, bring ye to the Lord glory and honour: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:8">95:8</a> bring to the Lord glory unto his name. Bring up sacrifices, and come into his courts: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:9">95:9</a> adore ye the Lord in his holy court. Let all the earth be moved at his presence. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:10">95:10</a> Say ye among the Gentiles, the Lord hath reigned. For he hath corrected the world, which shall not be moved: he will judge the people with justice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:11">95:11</a> Let the heavens rejoice, and let the earth be glad, let the sea be moved, and the fulness thereof: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:12">95:12</a> the fields and all things that are in them shall be joyful. Then shall all the trees of the woods rejoice </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:13">95:13</a> before the face of the Lord, because he cometh: because he cometh to judge the earth. He shall judge the world with justice, and the people with his truth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:1">96:1</a> For the same David, when his land was restored again to him. The Lord hath reigned, let the earth rejoice: let many islands be glad. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:2">96:2</a> Clouds and darkness are round about him: justice and judgment are the establishment of his throne. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:3">96:3</a> A fire shall go before him, and shall burn his enemies round about. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:4">96:4</a> His lightnings have shone forth to the world: the earth saw and trembled. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:5">96:5</a> The mountains melted like wax, at the presence of the Lord: at the presence of the Lord of all the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:6">96:6</a> The heavens declared his justice: and all people saw his glory. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:7">96:7</a> Let them be all confounded that adore graven things, and that glory in their idols. Adore him, all you his angels: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:8">96:8</a> Sion heard, and was glad. And the daughters of Juda rejoiced, because of thy judgments, O Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:9">96:9</a> For thou art the most high Lord over all the earth: thou art exalted exceedingly above all gods. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:10">96:10</a> You that love the Lord, hate evil: the Lord preserveth the souls of his saints, he will deliver them out of the hand of the sinner. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:11">96:11</a> Light is risen to the just, and joy to the right of heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:12">96:12</a> Rejoice, ye just, in the Lord: and give praise to the remembrance of his holiness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:1">97:1</a> A psalm for David himself. Sing ye to the Lord anew canticle: because he hath done wonderful things. His right hand hath wrought for him salvation, and his arm is holy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:2">97:2</a> The Lord hath made known his salvation: he hath revealed his justice in the sight of the Gentiles. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:3">97:3</a> He hath remembered his mercy his truth toward the house of Israel. All the ends of the earth have seen the salvation of our God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:4">97:4</a> Sing joyfully to God, all the earth; make melody, rejoice and sing. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:5">97:5</a> Sing praise to the Lord on the harp, on the harp, and with the voice of a psalm: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:6">97:6</a> with long trumpets, and sound of comet. Make a joyful noise before the Lord our king: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:7">97:7</a> let the sea be moved and the fulness thereof: the world end they that dwell therein. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:8">97:8</a> The rivers shall clap their hands, the mountains shall rejoice together </p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:9">97:9</a> at the presence of the Lord: because he cometh to judge the earth. He shall judge the world with justice, and the people with equity. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:1">98:1</a> A psalm for David himself. The Lord hath reigned, let the people be angry: he that sitteth on the cherubims: let the earth be moved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:2">98:2</a> The Lord is great in Sion, and high above all people. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:3">98:3</a> Let them give praise to thy great name: for it is terrible and holy: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:4">98:4</a> and the king's honour loveth judgment. Thou hast prepared directions: thou hast done judgment and justice in Jacob. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:5">98:5</a> Exalt ye the Lord our God, and adore his footstool, for it is holy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:6">98:6</a> Moses and Aaron among his priests: and Samuel among them that call upon his name. They called upon the Lord, and he heard them: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:7">98:7</a> he spoke to them in the pillar of the cloud. They kept his testimonies, and the commandment which he gave them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:8">98:8</a> Thou didst hear them, O Lord our God: thou wast a merciful God to them, and taking vengeance on all their inventions. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:9">98:9</a> Exalt ye the Lord our God, and adore at his holy mountain: for the Lord our God is holy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:1">99:1</a> A psalm of praise. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:2">99:2</a> Sing joyfully to God, all the earth: serve ye the Lord with gladness. Come in before his presence with exceeding great joy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:3">99:3</a> Know ye that the Lord he is God: he made us, and not we ourselves. We are his people and the sheep of his pasture. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:4">99:4</a> Go ye into his gates with praise, into his courts with hymns: and give glory to him. Praise ye his name: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:5">99:5</a> for the Lord is sweet, his mercy endureth for ever, and his truth to generation and generation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:1">100:1</a> A psalm for David himself. Mercy and judgment I will sing to thee, O Lord: I will sing, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:2">100:2</a> and I will understand in the unspotted way, when thou shalt come to me. I walked in the innocence of my heart, in the midst of my house. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:3">100:3</a> I did not set before my eyes any unjust thing: I hated the workers of iniquities. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:4">100:4</a> The perverse heart did not cleave to me: and the malignant, that turned aside from me, I would not know. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:5">100:5</a> The man that in private detracted his neighbour, him did I persecute. With him that had a proud eye, and an unsatiable heart, I would not eat. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:6">100:6</a> My eyes were upon the faithful of the earth, to sit with me: the man that walked in the perfect way, he served me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:7">100:7</a> He that worketh pride shall not dwell in the midst of my house: he that speaketh unjust things did not prosper before my eyes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:8">100:8</a> In the morning I put to death all the wicked of the land: that I might cut off all the workers of iniquity from the city of the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:1">101:1</a> The prayer of the poor man, when he was anxious, and poured out his supplication before the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:2">101:2</a> Hear, O Lord, my prayer: and let my cry come to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:3">101:3</a> Turn not away thy face from me: in the day when I am in trouble, incline thy ear to me. In what day soever I shall call upon thee, hear me speedily. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:4">101:4</a> For my days are vanished like smoke: and my bones are grown dry like fuel for the fire. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:5">101:5</a> I am smitten as grass, and my heart is withered: because I forgot to eat my bread. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:6">101:6</a> Through the voice of my groaning, my bone hath cleaved to my flesh. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:7">101:7</a> I am become like to a pelican of the wilderness: I am like a night raven in the house. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:8">101:8</a> I have watched, and am become as a sparrow all alone on the housetop. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:9">101:9</a> All the day long my enemies reproached me: and they that praised me did swear against me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:10">101:10</a> For I did eat ashes like bread, and mingled my drink with weeping. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:11">101:11</a> Because of thy anger and indignation: for having lifted me up thou hast thrown me down. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:12">101:12</a> My days have declined like a shadow, and I am withered like grass. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:13">101:13</a> But thou, O Lord, endurest for ever: and thy memorial to all generations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:14">101:14</a> Thou shalt arise and have mercy on Sion: for it is time to have mercy on it, for the time is come. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:15">101:15</a> For the stones thereof have pleased thy servants: and they shall have pity on the earth thereof. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:16">101:16</a> And the Gentiles shall fear thy name, O Lord, and all the kings of the earth thy glory. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:17">101:17</a> For the Lord hath built up Sion: and he shall be seen in his glory. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:18">101:18</a> He hath had regard to the prayer of the humble: and he hath not despised their petition. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:19">101:19</a> Let these things be written unto another generation: and the people that shall be created shall praise the Lord: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:20">101:20</a> Because he hath looked forth from his high sanctuary: from heaven the Lord hath looked upon the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:21">101:21</a> That he might hear the groans of them that are in fetters: that he might release the children of the slain: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:22">101:22</a> That they may declare the name of the Lord in Sion: and his praise in Jerusalem; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:23">101:23</a> When the people assemble together, and kings, to serve the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:24">101:24</a> He answered him in the way of his strength: Declare unto me the fewness of my days. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:25">101:25</a> Call me not away in the midst of my days: thy years are unto generation and generation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:26">101:26</a> In the beginning, O Lord, thou foundedst the earth: end the heavens are the works of thy hands. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:27">101:27</a> They shall perish but thou remainest: and all of them shall grow old like a garment: And as a vesture thou shalt change them, and they shall be changed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:28">101:28</a> But thou art always the selfsame, and thy years shall not fail. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:29">101:29</a> The children of thy servants shall continue: and their seed shall be directed for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:1">102:1</a> For David himself. Bless the Lord, O my soul: and let all that is within me bless his holy name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:2">102:2</a> Bless the Lord, O my soul, and never forget all he hath done for thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:3">102:3</a> Who forgiveth all thy iniquities: who healeth all thy diseases. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:4">102:4</a> Who redeemeth thy life from destruction: who crowneth thee with mercy and compassion. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:5">102:5</a> Who satisfieth thy desire with good things: thy youth shall be renewed like the eagle's. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:6">102:6</a> The Lord doth mercies, and judgment for all that suffer wrong. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:7">102:7</a> He hath made his ways known to Moses: his wills to the children of Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:8">102:8</a> The ford is compassionate and merciful: longsuffering and plenteous in mercy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:9">102:9</a> He will not always be angry: nor will he threaten for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:10">102:10</a> He hath not dealt with us according to our sins: nor rewarded us according to our iniquities. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:11">102:11</a> For according to the height of the heaven above the earth: he hath strengthened his mercy towards them that fear him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:12">102:12</a> As far as the east is from the west, so far hath he removed our iniquities from us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:13">102:13</a> As a father hath compassion on his children, so hath the Lord compassion on them that fear him: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:14">102:14</a> for he knoweth our frame. He remembereth that we are dust: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:15">102:15</a> man's days are as grass, as the flower of the field so shall he flourish. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:16">102:16</a> For the spirit shall pass in him, and he shall not be: and he shall know his place no more. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:17">102:17</a> But the mercy of the Lord is from eternity and unto eternity upon them that fear him: And his justice unto children's children, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:18">102:18</a> to such as keep his covenant, And are mindful of his commandments to do them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:19">102:19</a> The Lord hath prepared his throne in heaven: and his kingdom shall rule over all. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:20">102:20</a> Bless the Lord, all ye his angels: you that are mighty in strength, and execute his word, hearkening to the voice of his orders. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:21">102:21</a> Bless the Lord, all ye his hosts: you ministers of his that do his will. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:22">102:22</a> Bless the Lord, all his works: in every place of his dominion, O my soul, bless thou the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:1">103:1</a> For David himself. Bless the Lord, O my soul: O Lord my God, thou art exceedingly great. Thou hast put on praise and beauty: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:2">103:2</a> and art clothed with light as with a garment. Who stretchest out the heaven like a pavilion: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:3">103:3</a> who coverest the higher rooms thereof with water. Who makest the clouds thy chariot: who walkest upon the wings of the winds. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:4">103:4</a> Who makest thy angels spirits: and thy ministers a burning fire. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:5">103:5</a> Who hast founded the earth upon its own bases: it shall not be moved for ever and ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:6">103:6</a> The deep like a garment is its clothing: above the mountains shall the waters stand. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:7">103:7</a> At thy rebuke they shall flee: at the voice of thy thunder they shall fear. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:8">103:8</a> The mountains ascend, and the plains descend into the place which thou hast founded for them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:9">103:9</a> Thou hast set a bound which they shall not pass over; neither shall they return to cover the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:10">103:10</a> Thou sendest forth springs in the vales: between the midst of the hills the waters shall pass. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:11">103:11</a> All the beasts of the field shall drink: the wild asses shall expect in their thirst. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:12">103:12</a> Over them the birds of the air shall dwell: from the midst of the rocks they shall give forth their voices. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:13">103:13</a> Thou waterest the hills from thy upper rooms: the earth shall be filled with the fruit of thy works: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:14">103:14</a> Bringing forth grass for cattle, and herb for the service of men. That thou mayst bring bread out of the earth: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:15">103:15</a> and that wine may cheer the heart of man. That he may make the face cheerful with oil: and that bread may strengthen man's heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:16">103:16</a> The trees of the field shall be filled, and the cedars of Libanus which he hath planted: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:17">103:17</a> there the sparrows shall make their nests. The highest of them is the house of the heron. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:18">103:18</a> The high hills are a refuge for the harts, the rock for the irchins. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:19">103:19</a> He hath made the moon for seasons: the sun knoweth his going down. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:20">103:20</a> Thou hast appointed darkness, and it is night: in it shall all the beasts of the woods go about: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:21">103:21</a> The young lions roaring after their prey, and seeking their meat from God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:22">103:22</a> The sun ariseth, and they are gathered together: and they shall lie down in their dens. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:23">103:23</a> Man shall go forth to his work, and to his labour until the evening. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:24">103:24</a> How great are thy works, O Lord? thou hast made all things in wisdom: the earth is filled with thy riches. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:25">103:25</a> So is this great sea, which stretcheth wide its arms: there are creeping things without number: Creatures little and great. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:26">103:26</a> There the ships shall go. This sea dragon which thou hast formed to play therein. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:27">103:27</a> All expect of thee that thou give them food in season. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:28">103:28</a> What thou givest to them they shall gather up: when thou openest thy hand, they shall all be filled with good. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:29">103:29</a> But if thou turnest away thy face, they shall be troubled: thou shalt take away their breath, and they shall fail, and shall return to their dust. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:30">103:30</a> Thou shalt send forth thy spirit, and they shall be created: and thou shalt renew the face of the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:31">103:31</a> May the glory of the Lord endure for ever: the Lord shall rejoice in his works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:32">103:32</a> He looketh upon the earth, and maketh it tremble: he toucheth the mountains, and they smoke. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:33">103:33</a> I will sing to the Lord as long as I live: I will sing praise to my God while I have my being. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:34">103:34</a> Let my speech be acceptable to him: but I will take delight in the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:35">103:35</a> Let sinners be consumed out of the earth, and the unjust, so that they be no more: O my soul, bless thou the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:1">104:1</a> Alleluia. Give glory to the Lord, and call upon his name: declare his deeds among the Gentiles. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:2">104:2</a> Sing to him, yea sing praises to him: relate all his wondrous works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:3">104:3</a> Glory ye in his holy name: let the heart of them rejoice that seek the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:4">104:4</a> Seek ye the Lord, and be strengthened: seek his face evermore. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:5">104:5</a> Remember his marvellous works which he hath done; his wonders, and the judgments of his mouth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:6">104:6</a> O ye seed of Abraham his servant; ye sons of Jacob his chosen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:7">104:7</a> He is the Lord our God: his judgments are in all the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:8">104:8</a> He hath remembered his covenant for ever: the word which he commanded to a thousand generations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:9">104:9</a> Which he made to Abraham; and his oath to Isaac: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:10">104:10</a> And he appointed the same to Jacob for a law, and to Israel for an everlasting testament: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:11">104:11</a> Saying: To thee will I give the land of Chanaan, the lot of your inheritance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:12">104:12</a> When they were but a small number: yea very few, and sojourners therein: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:13">104:13</a> And they passed from nation to nation, and from one kingdom to another people. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:14">104:14</a> He suffered no man to hurt them: and he reproved kings for their sakes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:15">104:15</a> Touch ye not my anointed: and do no evil to my prophets. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:16">104:16</a> And he called a famine upon the land: and he broke in pieces all the support of bread. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:17">104:17</a> He sent a man before them: Joseph, who was sold for a slave. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:18">104:18</a> They humbled his feet in fetters: the iron pierced his soul, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:19">104:19</a> until his word came. The word of the Lord inflamed him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:20">104:20</a> The king sent, and he released him: the ruler of the people, and he set him at liberty. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:21">104:21</a> He made him master of his house, and ruler of all his possession. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:22">104:22</a> That he might instruct his princes as himself, and teach his ancients wisdom. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:23">104:23</a> And Israel went into Egypt: and Jacob was a sojourner in the land of Cham. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:24">104:24</a> And he increased his people exceedingly: and strengthened them over their enemies, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:25">104:25</a> He turned their heart to hate his people: and to deal deceitfully with his servants. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:26">104:26</a> He sent Moses his servant: Aaron the man whom he had chosen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:27">104:27</a> He gave them power to shew his signs, and his wonders in the land of Cham. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:28">104:28</a> He sent darkness, and made it obscure: and grieved not his words. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:29">104:29</a> He turned their waters into blood, and destroyed their fish. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:30">104:30</a> Their land brought forth frogs, in the inner chambers of their kings. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:31">104:31</a> He spoke, and there came divers sorts of flies and sciniphs in all their coasts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:32">104:32</a> He gave them hail for rain, a burning fire in the land. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:33">104:33</a> And he destroyed their vineyards and their fig trees: and he broke in pieces the trees of their coasts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:34">104:34</a> He spoke, and the locust came, and the bruchus, of which there was no number. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:35">104:35</a> And they devoured all the grass in their land, and consumed all the fruit of their ground. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:36">104:36</a> And he slew all the firstborn in their land: the firstfruits of all their labour. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:37">104:37</a> And he brought them out with silver and gold: and there was not among their tribes one that was feeble. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:38">104:38</a> Egypt was glad when they departed: for the fear of them lay upon them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:39">104:39</a> He spread a cloud for their protection, and fire to give them light in the night. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:40">104:40</a> They asked, and the quail came: and he filled them with the bread of heaven. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:41">104:41</a> He opened the rock, and waters flowed: rivers ran down in the dry land. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:42">104:42</a> Because he remembered his holy word, which he had spoken to his servant Abraham. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:43">104:43</a> And he brought forth his people with joy, and his chosen with gladness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:44">104:44</a> And he gave them the lands of the Gentiles: and they possessed the labours of the people: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:45">104:45</a> That they might observe his justifications, and seek after his law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:1">105:1</a> Alleluia. Give glory to the Lord, for he is good: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:2">105:2</a> Who shall declare the powers of the Lord? who shall set forth all his praises? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:3">105:3</a> Blessed are they that keep judgment, and do justice at all times. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:4">105:4</a> Remember us, O Lord, in the favour of thy people: visit us with thy salvation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:5">105:5</a> That we may see the good of thy chosen, that we may rejoice in the joy of thy nation: that thou mayst be praised with thy inheritance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:6">105:6</a> We have sinned with our fathers: we have acted unjustly, we have wrought iniquity. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:7">105:7</a> Our fathers understood not thy wonders in Egypt: they remembered not the multitude of thy mercies: And they provoked to wrath going up to the sea, even the Red Sea. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:8">105:8</a> And he saved them for his own name's sake: that he might make his power known. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:9">105:9</a> And he rebuked the Red Sea, and it was dried up: and he led them through the depths, as in a wilderness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:10">105:10</a> And he saved them from the hand of them that hated them: and he redeemed them from the hand of the enemy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:11">105:11</a> And the water covered them that afflicted them: there was not one of them left. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:12">105:12</a> And they believed his words: and they sang his praises. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:13">105:13</a> They had quickly done, they forgot his works: and they waited not for his counsels. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:14">105:14</a> And they coveted their desire in the desert: and they tempted God in the place without water. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:15">105:15</a> And he gave them their request: and sent fulness into their souls. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:16">105:16</a> And they provoked Moses in the camp, Aaron the holy one of the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:17">105:17</a> The earth opened and swallowed up Dathan: and covered the congregation of Abiron. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:18">105:18</a> And a fire was kindled in their congregation: the flame burned the wicked. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:19">105:19</a> They made also a calf in Horeb: and they adored the graven thing. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:20">105:20</a> And they changed their glory into the likeness of a calf that eateth grass. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:21">105:21</a> They forgot God, who saved them, who had done great things in Egypt, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:22">105:22</a> wondrous works in the land of Cham: terrible things in the Red Sea. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:23">105:23</a> And he said that he would destroy them: had not Moses his chosen stood before him in the breach: To turn away his wrath, lest he should destroy them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:24">105:24</a> And they set at nought the desirable land. They believed not his word, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:25">105:25</a> and they murmured in their tents: they hearkened not to the voice of the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:26">105:26</a> And he lifted up his hand over them: to overthrow them in the desert; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:27">105:27</a> And to cast down their seed among the nations, and to scatter them in the countries. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:28">105:28</a> They also were initiated to Beelphegor: and ate the sacrifices of the dead. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:29">105:29</a> And they provoked him with their inventions: and destruction was multiplied among them. </p>
