 <p><a name="an_105:30">105:30</a> Then Phinees stood up, and pacified him: and the slaughter ceased. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:31">105:31</a> And it was reputed to him unto justice, to generation and generation for evermore. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:32">105:32</a> They provoked him also at the waters of contradiction: and Moses was afflicted for their sakes: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:33">105:33</a> because they exasperated his spirit. And he distinguished with his lips. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:34">105:34</a> They did not destroy the nations of which the Lord spoke unto them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:35">105:35</a> And they were mingled among the heathens, and learned their works: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:36">105:36</a> and served their idols, and it became a stumblingblock to them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:37">105:37</a> And they sacrificed their sons, and their daughters to devils. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:38">105:38</a> And they shed innocent blood: the blood of their sons and of their daughters which they sacrificed to the idols of Chanaan. And the land was polluted with blood, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:39">105:39</a> and was defiled with their works: and they went aside after their own inventions. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:40">105:40</a> And the Lord was exceedingly angry with his people: and he abhorred his inheritance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:41">105:41</a> And he delivered them into the hands of the nations: and they that hated them had dominion over them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:42">105:42</a> And their enemies afflicted them: and they were humbled under their hands: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:43">105:43</a> many times did he deliver them. But they provoked him with their counsel: and they were brought low by their iniquities. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:44">105:44</a> And he saw when they were in tribulation: and he heard their prayer. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:45">105:45</a> And he was mindful of his covenant: and repented according to the multitude of his mercies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:46">105:46</a> And he gave them unto mercies, in the sight of all those that had made them captives. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:47">105:47</a> Save us, O Lord, our God: and gather us from among nations: That we may give thanks to thy holy name, and may glory in thy praise. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:48">105:48</a> Blessed be the Lord the God of Israel, from everlasting to everlasting: and let all the people say: So be it, so be it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:1">106:1</a> Give glory to the Lord, for he is good: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:2">106:2</a> Let them say so that have been redeemed by the Lord, whom he hath redeemed from the hand of the enemy: and gathered out of the countries. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:3">106:3</a> From the rising and the setting of the sun, from the north and from the sea. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:4">106:4</a> They wandered in a wilderness, in a place without water: they found not the way of a city for their habitation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:5">106:5</a> They were hungry and thirsty: their soul fainted in them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:6">106:6</a> And they cried to the Lord in their tribulation: and he delivered them out of their distresses. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:7">106:7</a> And he led them into the right way: that they might go to a city of habitation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:8">106:8</a> Let the mercies of the Lord give glory to him: and his wonderful works to the children of men. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:9">106:9</a> For he hath satisfied the empty soul, and hath filled the hungry soul with good things. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:10">106:10</a> Such as sat in darkness and in the shadow of death: bound in want and in iron. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:11">106:11</a> Because they had exasperated the words of God: and provoked the counsel of the most High: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:12">106:12</a> And their heart was humbled with labours: they were weakened, and their was none to help them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:13">106:13</a> Then they cried to the Lord in their affliction: and he delivered them out of their distresses. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:14">106:14</a> And he brought them out of darkness, and the shadow of death; and broke their bonds in sunder. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:15">106:15</a> Let the mercies of the Lord give glory to him, and his wonderful works to the children of men. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:16">106:16</a> Because he hath broken gates of brass, and burst the iron bars. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:17">106:17</a> He took them out of the way of their iniquity: for they were brought low for their injustices. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:18">106:18</a> Their soul abhorred all manner of meat: and they drew nigh even to the gates of death. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:19">106:19</a> And they cried to the Lord in their affliction: and he delivered them out of their distresses. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:20">106:20</a> He sent his word, and healed them: and delivered them from their destructions. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:21">106:21</a> Let the mercies of the Lord give glory to him: and his wonderful works to the children of men. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:22">106:22</a> And let them sacrifice the sacrifice of praise: and declare his works with joy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:23">106:23</a> They that go down to the sea in ships, doing business in the great waters: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:24">106:24</a> These have seen the works of the Lord, and his wonders in the deep. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:25">106:25</a> He said the word, and there arose a storm of wind: and the waves thereof were lifted up. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:26">106:26</a> They mount up to the heavens, and they go down to the depths: their soul pined away with evils. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:27">106:27</a> They were troubled, and reeled like a drunken man; and all their wisdom was swallowed up. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:28">106:28</a> And they cried to the Lord in their affliction: and he brought them out of their distresses. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:29">106:29</a> And he turned the storm into a breeze: and its waves were still. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:30">106:30</a> And they rejoiced because they were still: and he brought them to the haven which they wished for. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:31">106:31</a> Let the mercies of the Lord give glory to him, and his wonderful works to the children of men. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:32">106:32</a> And let them exalt him in the church of the people: and praise him in the chair of the ancients. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:33">106:33</a> He hath turned rivers into a wilderness: and the sources of water into dry ground: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:34">106:34</a> A fruitful land into barrenness, for the wickedness of them that dwell therein. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:35">106:35</a> He hath turned a wilderness into pools of water, and a dry land into water springs. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:36">106:36</a> And hath placed there the hungry; and they made a city for their habitation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:37">106:37</a> And they sowed fields, and planted vineyards: and they yielded fruit of birth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:38">106:38</a> And he blessed them, and they were multiplied exceedingly: and their cattle he suffered not to decrease. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:39">106:39</a> Then they were brought to be few: and they were afflicted through the trouble of evils and sorrow. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:40">106:40</a> Contempt was poured forth upon their princes: and he caused them to wander where there was no passing, and out of the way. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:41">106:41</a> And he helped the poor out of poverty: and made him families like a flock of sheep. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:42">106:42</a> The just shall see, and shall rejoice, and all iniquity shall stop their mouth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:43">106:43</a> Who is wise, and will keep these things: and will understand the mercies of the Lord? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:1">107:1</a> A canticle of a psalm for David himself. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:2">107:2</a> My heart is ready, O God, my heart is ready: I will sing, and will give praise, with my glory. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:3">107:3</a> Arise, my glory; arise, psaltery and harp: I will arise in the morning early. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:4">107:4</a> I will praise thee, O Lord, among the people: and I will sing unto thee among the populations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:5">107:5</a> For thy mercy is great above the heavens: and thy truth even unto the clouds. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:6">107:6</a> Be thou exalted, O God, above the heavens, and thy glory over all the earth: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:7">107:7</a> that thy beloved may be delivered. Save with thy right hand and hear me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:8">107:8</a> God hath spoken in his holiness. I will rejoice, and I will divide Sichem and I will mete out the vale of tabernacles. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:9">107:9</a> Galaad is mine, and Manasses is mine and Ephraim the protection of my head. Juda is my king: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:10">107:10</a> Moab the pot of my hope. Over Edom I will stretch out my shoe: the aliens are become my friends. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:11">107:11</a> Who will bring me into the strong city? who will lead me into Edom? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:12">107:12</a> Wilt not thou, O God, who hast cast us off? and wilt not thou, O God, go forth with our armies? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:13">107:13</a> O grant us help from trouble: for vain is the help of man. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:14">107:14</a> Through God we shall do mightily: and he will bring our enemies to nothing. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:1">108:1</a> Unto the end, a psalm for David. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:2">108:2</a> O God, be not thou silent in thy praise: for the mouth of the wicked and the mouth of the deceitful man is opened against me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:3">108:3</a> They have spoken against with deceitful tongues; and they have compassed me about with words of hatred; and have fought against me without cause. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:4">108:4</a> Instead of making me a return of love, they detracted me: but I gave myself to prayer. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:5">108:5</a> And they repaid me evil for good: and hatred for my love. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:6">108:6</a> Set thou the sinner over him: and may the devil stand at his right hand. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:7">108:7</a> When he is judged, may he go out condemned; and may his prayer be turned to sin. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:8">108:8</a> May his days be few: and his bishopric let another take. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:9">108:9</a> May his children be fatherless, and his wife a widow. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:10">108:10</a> Let his children be carried about vagabonds, and beg; and let them be cast out of their dwellings. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:11">108:11</a> May the userer search all his substance: and let strangers plunder his labours. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:12">108:12</a> May there be none to help him: nor none to pity his fatherless offspring. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:13">108:13</a> May his posterity be cut off; in one generation may his name be blotted out. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:14">108:14</a> May the iniquity of his fathers be remembered in the sight of the Lord: and let not the sin of his mother be blotted out. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:15">108:15</a> May they be before the lord continually, and let the memory of them perish from the earth: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:16">108:16</a> because he remembered not to show mercy, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:17">108:17</a> But persecuted the poor man and the beggar; and the broken in heart, to put him to death. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:18">108:18</a> And he loved cursing, and it shall come unto him: and he would not have blessing, and it shall be far from him. And he put on cursing, like a garment: and it went in like water into his entrails, and like oil in his bones. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:19">108:19</a> May it be unto him like a garment which covereth him; and like a girdle with which he is girded continually. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:20">108:20</a> This is the work of them who detract me before the Lord; and who speak evils against my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:21">108:21</a> But thou, O Lord, do with for thy names sake: because thy mercy is sweet. Do thou deliver me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:22">108:22</a> for I am poor and needy, and my heart is troubled within me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:23">108:23</a> I am taken away like the shadow when it declineth: and I am shaken off as locusts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:24">108:24</a> My knees are weakened through fasting: and my flesh is changed for oil. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:25">108:25</a> And I am become a reproach to them: they saw me and they shaked their heads, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:26">108:26</a> Help me, O Lord my God; save me according to thy mercy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:27">108:27</a> And let them know that this is thy hand: and that thou, O Lord, hast done it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:28">108:28</a> They will curse and thou will bless: let them that rise up against me be confounded: but thy servant shall rejoice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:29">108:29</a> Let them that detract me be clothed with shame: and let them be covered with the their confusion as with a double cloak. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:30">108:30</a> I will give great thanks to the Lord with my mouth: and in the midst of many I will praise him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:31">108:31</a> Because he hath stood at the right hand of the poor, to save my soul from persecutors </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:1">109:1</a> The Lord said to my Lord: Sit thou at my right hand: Until I make thy enemies thy footstool. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:2">109:2</a> The Lord will send forth the sceptre of thy power out of Sion: rule thou in the midst of thy enemies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:3">109:3</a> With thee is the principality in the day of thy strength: in the brightness of the saints: from the womb before the day star I begot thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:4">109:4</a> The Lord hath sworn, and he will not repent: Thou art a priest for ever according to the order of Melchisedech. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:5">109:5</a> The Lord at thy right hand hath broken kings in the day of his wrath. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:6">109:6</a> He shall judge among nations, he shall fill ruins: he shall crush the heads in the land of the many. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:7">109:7</a> He shall drink of the torrent in the way: therefore shall he lift up the head. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:1">110:1</a> I will praise thee, O Lord, with my whole heart; in the council of the just: and in the congregation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:2">110:2</a> Great are the works of the Lord: sought out according to all his wills </p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:3">110:3</a> His work is praise and magnificence: and his justice continueth for ever and ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:4">110:4</a> He hath made a remembrance of his wonderful works, being a merciful and gracious Lord: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:5">110:5</a> he hath given food to them that fear him. He will be mindful for ever of his covenant: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:6">110:6</a> he will shew forth to his people the power of his works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:7">110:7</a> That he may give them the inheritance of the Gentiles: the works of his hands are truth and judgment. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:8">110:8</a> All his commandments are faithful: confirmed for ever and ever, made in truth and equity. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:9">110:9</a> He hath sent redemption to his people: he hath commanded his covenant for ever. Holy and terrible is his name: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:10">110:10</a> the fear of the Lord is the beginning of wisdom. A good understanding to all that do it: his praise continueth for ever and ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:1">111:1</a> Blessed is the man that feareth the Lord: he shall delight exceedingly in his commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:2">111:2</a> His seed shall be mighty upon earth: the generation of the righteous shall be blessed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:3">111:3</a> Glory and wealth shall be in his house: and his justice remaineth for ever and ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:4">111:4</a> To the righteous a light is risen up in darkness: he is merciful, and compassionate and just. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:5">111:5</a> Acceptable is the man that showeth mercy and lendeth: he shall order his words with judgment: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:6">111:6</a> because he shall not be moved for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:7">111:7</a> The just shall be in everlasting remembrance: he shall not hear the evil hearing. His heart is ready to hope in the Lord: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:8">111:8</a> his heart is strengthened, he shall not be moved until he look over his enemies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:9">111:9</a> He hath distributed, he hath given to the poor: his justice remaineth for ever and ever: his horn shall be exalted in glory. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:10">111:10</a> The wicked shall see, and shall be angry, he shall gnash with his teeth and pine away: the desire of the wicked shall perish. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:1">112:1</a> Praise the Lord, ye children: praise ye the name of the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:2">112:2</a> Blessed be the name of the Lord, from henceforth now and for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:3">112:3</a> From the rising of the sun unto the going down of the same, the name of the Lord is worthy of praise. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:4">112:4</a> The Lord is high above all nations; and his glory above the heavens. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:5">112:5</a> Who is as the Lord our God, who dwelleth on high: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:6">112:6</a> and looketh down on the low things in heaven and in earth? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:7">112:7</a> Raising up the needy from the earth, and lifting up the poor out of the dunghill:: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:8">112:8</a> That he may place him with princes, with the princes of his people. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:9">112:9</a> Who maketh a barren woman to dwell in a house, the joyful mother of children. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:1">113:1</a> When Israel went out of Egypt, the house of Jacob from a barbarous people: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:2">113:2</a> Judea made his sanctuary, Israel his dominion. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:3">113:3</a> The sea saw and fled: Jordan was turned back. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:4">113:4</a> The mountains skipped like rams, and the hills like the lambs of the flock. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:5">113:5</a> What ailed thee, O thou sea, that thou didst flee: and thou, O Jordan, that thou wast turned back? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:6">113:6</a> Ye mountains, that ye skipped like rams, and ye hills, like lambs of the flock? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:7">113:7</a> At the presence of the Lord the earth was moved, at the presence of the God of Jacob: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:8">113:8</a> Who turned the rock into pools of water, and the stony hill into fountains of waters. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:9">113:9</a> Not to us, O Lord, not to us; but to thy name give glory. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:10">113:10</a> For thy mercy, and for thy truth's sake: lest the gentiles should say: Where is their God? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:11">113:11</a> But our God is in heaven: he hath done all things whatsoever he would. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:12">113:12</a> The idols of the gentiles are silver and gold, the works of the hands of men. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:13">113:13</a> They have mouths and speak not: they have eyes and see not. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:14">113:14</a> They have ears and hear not: they have noses and smell not. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:15">113:15</a> They have hands and feel not: they have feet and walk not: neither shall they cry out through their throat. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:16">113:16</a> Let them that make them become like unto them: and all such as trust in them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:17">113:17</a> The house of Israel hath hoped in the Lord: he is their helper and their protector. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:18">113:18</a> The house of Aaron hath hoped in the Lord: he is their helper and their protector. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:19">113:19</a> They that fear the Lord hath hoped in the Lord: he is their helper and their protector. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:20">113:20</a> The Lord hath been mindful of us, and hath blessed us. He hath blessed the house of Israel: he hath blessed the house of Aaron. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:21">113:21</a> He hath blessed all that fear the Lord, both little and great. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:22">113:22</a> May the Lord add blessings upon you: upon you, and upon your children. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:23">113:23</a> Blessed be you of the Lord, who made heaven and earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:24">113:24</a> The heaven of heaven is the Lord's: but the earth he has given to the children of men. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:25">113:25</a> The dead shall not praise thee, O Lord: nor any of them that go down to hell. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:26">113:26</a> But we that live bless the Lord: from this time now and for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:1">114:1</a> I have loved, because the Lord will hear the voice of my prayer. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:2">114:2</a> Because he hath inclined his ear unto me: and in my days I will call upon him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:3">114:3</a> The sorrows of death have encompassed me: and the perils of hell have found me. I met with trouble and sorrow: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:4">114:4</a> and I called upon the name of the Lord. O Lord, deliver my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:5">114:5</a> The Lord is merciful and just, and our God sheweth mercy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:6">114:6</a> The Lord is the keeper of little ones: I was little and he delivered me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:7">114:7</a> Turn, O my soul, into thy rest: for the Lord hath been bountiful to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:8">114:8</a> For he hath delivered my soul from death: my eyes from tears, my feet from falling. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:9">114:9</a> I will please the Lord in the land of the living. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:10">115:10</a> I have believed, therefore have I spoken; but I have been humbled exceedingly. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:11">115:11</a> I said in my excess: Every man is a liar. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:12">115:12</a> What shall I render to the Lord, for all the things he hath rendered unto me? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:13">115:13</a> I will take the chalice of salvation; and I will call upon the name of the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:14">115:14</a> I will pay my vows to the Lord before all his people: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:15">115:15</a> precious in the sight of the Lord is the death of his saints. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:16">115:16</a> O Lord, for I am thy servant: I am thy servant, and the son of thy handmaid. Thou hast broken my bonds: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:17">115:17</a> I will sacrifice to thee the sacrifice of praise, and I will call upon the name of the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:18">115:18</a> I will pay my vows to the Lord in the sight of all his people: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:19">115:19</a> in the courts of the house of the Lord, in the midst of thee, O Jerusalem. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:1">116:1</a> O praise the Lord, all ye nations: praise him, all ye people. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:2">116:2</a> For his mercy is confirmed upon us: and the truth of the Lord remaineth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:1">117:1</a> Give praise to Lord, for he is good: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:2">117:2</a> Let Israel now say that he is good: that his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:3">117:3</a> Let the house of Aaron now say, that his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:4">117:4</a> Let them that fear the Lord now say, that his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:5">117:5</a> In my trouble I called upon the Lord: and the Lord heard me, and enlarged me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:6">117:6</a> The Lord is my helper, I will not fear what man can do unto me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:7">117:7</a> The Lord is my helper: and I will look over my enemies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:8">117:8</a> It is good to confide in the Lord, rather than to have confidence in man. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:9">117:9</a> It is good to trust in the Lord, rather than to trust in princes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:10">117:10</a> All nations compassed me about; and in the name of the Lord I have been revenged on them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:11">117:11</a> Surrounding me they compassed me about: and in the name of the Lord I have been revenged on them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:12">117:12</a> They surrounded me like bees, and they burned like fire among thorns: and in the name of the Lord I was revenged on them </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:13">117:13</a> Being pushed I was overturned that I might fall: but the Lord supported me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:14">117:14</a> The Lord is my strength and my praise: and he is become my salvation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:15">117:15</a> The voice of rejoicing and of salvation is in the tabernacles of the just. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:16">117:16</a> The right hand of the Lord hath wrought strength: the right hand of the Lord hath exulted me: the right hand of the Lord hath wrought strength. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:17">117:17</a> I shall not die, but live: and shall declare the works of the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:18">117:18</a> The Lord chastising hath chastised me: but he hath not delivered me over to death. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:19">117:19</a> Open ye to me the gates of justice: I will go into them, and give praise to the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:20">117:20</a> This is the gate of the Lord, the just shall enter into it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:21">117:21</a> I will give glory to thee because thou hast heard me: and art become my salvation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:22">117:22</a> The stone which the builders rejected; the same is become the head of the corner. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:23">117:23</a> This is the Lord's doing: and it is wonderful in our eyes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:24">117:24</a> This is the day which the Lord hath made: let us be glad and rejoice therein. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:25">117:25</a> O Lord, save me: O Lord, give good success. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:26">117:26</a> Blessed be he that cometh in the name Lord. We have blessed you out of the house of the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:27">117:27</a> The Lord is God, and he hath shone upon us. Appoint a solemn day, with shady boughs, even to the horn of the alter. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:28">117:28</a> Thou art my God, and I will praise thee: thou art my God, and I will exalt thee. I will praise thee, because thou hast heard me, and art become my salvation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:29">117:29</a> O praise ye the Lord, for he is good: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:1">118:1</a> [ALEPH] Blessed are the undefiled in the way, who walk in the law of the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:2">118:2</a> Blessed are they who search his testimonies: that seek him with their whole heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:3">118:3</a> For they that work iniquity, have not walked in his ways. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:4">118:4</a> Thou hast commanded thy commandments to be kept most diligently. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:5">118:5</a> O! that my ways may be directed to keep thy justifications. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:6">118:6</a> Then shall I not be confounded, when I shall look into all thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:7">118:7</a> I will praise thee with uprightness of heart, when I shall have learned the judgments of thy justice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:8">118:8</a> I will keep thy justifications: O! do not thou utterly forsake me.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:9">118:9</a> [BETH] By what doth a young man correct his way? by observing thy words. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:10">118:10</a> With my whole heart have I sought after thee: let me not stray from thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:11">118:11</a> Thy words have I hidden in my heart, that I may not sin against thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:12">118:12</a> Blessed art thou, O Lord: teach me thy justifications. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:13">118:13</a> With my lips I have pronounced all the judgments of thy mouth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:14">118:14</a> I have been delighted in the way of thy testimonies, as in all riches. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:15">118:15</a> I will meditate on thy commandments: and I will consider thy ways. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:16">118:16</a> I will think of thy justifications: I will not forget thy words.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:17">118:17</a> [GIMEL] Give bountifully to thy servant, enliven me: and I shall keep thy words. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:18">118:18</a> Open thou my eyes: and I will consider the wondrous things of thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:19">118:19</a> I am a sojourner on the earth: hide not thy commandments from me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:20">118:20</a> My soul hath coveted to long for thy justifications, at all times. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:21">118:21</a> Thou hast rebuked the proud: they are cursed who decline from thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:22">118:22</a> Remove from reproach and contempt: because I have sought after thy testimonies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:23">118:23</a> For princes sat, and spoke against me: but thy servant was employed in thy justifications. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:24">118:24</a> For thy testimonies are my meditation: and thy justifications my counsel.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:25">118:25</a> [DALETH] My soul hath cleaved to the pavement: quicken thou me according to thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:26">118:26</a> I have declared my ways, and thou hast heard me: tech me thy justifications. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:27">118:27</a> Make me to understand the way of thy justifications: and I shall be exercised in thy wondrous works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:28">118:28</a> My soul hath slumbered through heaviness: strengthen thou me in thy words. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:29">118:29</a> Remove from me the way of iniquity: and out of thy law have mercy on me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:30">118:30</a> I have chosen the way of truth: thy judgments I have not forgotten. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:31">118:31</a> I have stuck to thy testimonies, O Lord: put me not to shame. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:32">118:32</a> I have run the way of thy commandments, when thou didst enlarge my heart.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:33">118:33</a> [HE] Set before me for a law the way of thy justifications, O Lord: and I will always seek after it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:34">118:34</a> Give me understanding, and I will search thy law ; and I will keep it with my whole heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:35">118:35</a> Lead me into the path of thy commandments; for this same I have desired. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:36">118:36</a> Incline my heart into thy testimonies and not to covetousness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:37">118:37</a> Turn away my eyes that they may not behold vanity: quicken me in thy way. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:38">118:38</a> Establish thy word to thy servant, in thy fear. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:39">118:39</a> Turn away my reproach, which I have apprehended: for thy judgments are delightful. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:40">118:40</a> Behold I have longed after thy precepts: quicken me in thy justice.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:41">118:41</a> [VAU] Let thy mercy also come upon me, O Lord: thy salvation according to thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:42">118:42</a> So shall I answer them that reproach me in any thing; that I have trusted in thy words. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:43">118:43</a> And take not thou the word of truth utterly out of my mouth: for in thy words have I hoped exceedingly. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:44">118:44</a> So shall I always keep thy law, for ever and ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:45">118:45</a> And I walked at large: because I have sought after thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:46">118:46</a> And I spoke of thy testimonies before kings: and I was not ashamed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:47">118:47</a> I meditated also on thy commandments, which I loved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:48">118:48</a> And I lifted up my hands to thy commandments, which I loved: and I was exercised in thy justifications.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:49">118:49</a> [ZAIN] Be thou mindful of thy word to thy servant, in which thou hast given me hope. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:50">118:50</a> This hath comforted me in my humiliation: because thy word hath enlivened me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:51">118:51</a> The proud did iniquitously altogether: but I declined not from thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:52">118:52</a> I remembered, O Lord, thy judgments of old: and I was comforted. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:53">118:53</a> A fainting hath taken hold of me, because of the wicked that forsake thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:54">118:54</a> Thy justifications were the subject of my song, in the place of my pilgrimage. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:55">118:55</a> In the night I have remembered thy name, O Lord: and have kept thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:56">118:56</a> This happened to me: because I sought after thy justifications.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:57">118:57</a> [HETH] O Lord, my portion, I have said, I would keep the law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:58">118:58</a> I entreated thy face with all my heart: have mercy on me according to thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:59">118:59</a> I have thought on my ways: and turned my feet unto thy testimonies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:60">118:60</a> I am ready, and am not troubled: that I may keep thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:61">118:61</a> The cords of the wicked have encompassed me: but I have not forgotten thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:62">118:62</a> I rose at midnight to give praise to thee; for the judgments of thy justification. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:63">118:63</a> I am a partaker with all them that fear thee, and that keep thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:64">118:64</a> The earth, O Lord, is full of thy mercy: teach me thy justifications.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:65">118:65</a> [TETH] Thou hast done well with thy servant, O Lord, according to thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:66">118:66</a> Teach me goodness and discipline and knowledge; for I have believed thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:67">118:67</a> Before I was humbled I offended; therefore have I kept thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:68">118:68</a> Thou art good; and in thy goodness teach me thy justifications. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:69">118:69</a> The iniquity of the proud hath been multiplied over me: but I will seek thy commandments with my whole heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:70">118:70</a> Their heart is curdled like milk: but I have meditated on thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:71">118:71</a> It is good for me that thou hast humbled me, that I may learn thy justifications. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:72">118:72</a> The law of thy mouth is good to me, above thousands of gold and silver.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:73">118:73</a> [JOD] Thy hands have made me and formed me: give me understanding, and I will learn thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:74">118:74</a> They that fear thee shall see me, and shall be glad: because I have greatly hoped in thy words. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:75">118:75</a> I know, O Lord, that thy judgments are equity: and in thy truth thou hast humbled me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:76">118:76</a> O! let thy mercy be for my comfort, according to thy word unto thy servant. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:77">118:77</a> Let thy tender mercies come unto me, and I shall live: for thy law is my meditation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:78">118:78</a> Let the proud be ashamed, because they have done unjustly towards me: but I will be employed in thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:79">118:79</a> Let them that fear thee turn to me" and they that know thy testimonies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:80">118:80</a> Let my heart be undefiled in thy justifications, that I may not be confounded.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:81">118:81</a> [CAPH] My soul hath fainted after thy salvation: and in thy word I have very much hoped. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:82">118:82</a> My eyes have failed for thy word, saying: When wilt thou comfort me? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:83">118:83</a> For I am become like a bottle in the frost: I have not forgotten thy justifications. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:84">118:84</a> How many are the days of thy servant: when wilt thou execute judgment on them that persecute me? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:85">118:85</a> The wicked have told me fables: but not as thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:86">118:86</a> All thy statutes are truth: they have persecuted me unjustly, do thou help me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:87">118:87</a> They had almost made an end of me upon earth: but I have not forsaken thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:88">118:88</a> Quicken thou me according to thy mercy: and I shall keep the testimonies of thy mouth.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:89">118:89</a> [LAMED] For ever, O Lord, thy word standeth firm in heaven. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:90">118:90</a> Thy truth unto all generations: thou hast founded the earth, and it continueth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:91">118:91</a> By thy ordinance the day goeth on: for all things serve thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:92">118:92</a> Unless thy law had been my meditation, I had then perhaps perished in my abjection. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:93">118:93</a> Thy justifications I will never forget: for by them thou hast given me life. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:94">118:94</a> I am thine, save thou me: for I have sought thy justifications. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:95">118:95</a> The wicked have waited for me to destroy me: but I have understood thy testimonies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:96">118:96</a> I have seen an end to all persecution: thy commandment is exceeding broad.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:97">118:97</a> [MEM] O how have I loved thy law, O Lord! it is my meditation all the day. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:98">118:98</a> Through thy commandment, thou hast made me wiser than my enemies: for it is ever with me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:99">118:99</a> I have understood more than all my teachers: because thy testimonies are my meditation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:100">118:100</a> I have had understanding above ancients: because I have sought thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:101">118:101</a> I have restrained my feet from every evil way: that I may keep thy words. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:102">118:102</a> I have not declined from thy judgments, because thou hast set me a law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:103">118:103</a> How sweet are thy words to my palate! more than honey to my mouth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:104">118:104</a> By thy commandments I have had understanding: therefore have I hated every way of iniquity.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:105">118:105</a> [NUN] Thy word is a lamp to my feet, and a light to my paths. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:106">118:106</a> I have sworn and am determined to keep the judgments of thy justice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:107">118:107</a> I have been humbled, O Lord, exceedingly: quicken thou me according to thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:108">118:108</a> The free offerings of my mouth make acceptable, O Lord: and teach me thy judgments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:109">118:109</a> My soul is continually in my hands: and I have not forgotten thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:110">118:110</a> Sinners have laid a snare for me: but I have not erred from thy precepts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:111">118:111</a> I have purchased thy testimonies for an inheritance for ever: because they are a joy to my heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:112">118:112</a> I have inclined my heart to do thy justifications for ever, for the reward.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:113">118:113</a> [SAMECH] I have hated the unjust: and have loved thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:114">118:114</a> Thou art my helper and my protector: and in thy word I have greatly hoped. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:115">118:115</a> Depart from me, ye malignant: and I will search the commandments of my God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:116">118:116</a> Uphold me according to thy word, and I shall live: and let me not be confounded in my expectation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:117">118:117</a> Help me, and I shall be saved: and I will meditate always on thy justifications. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:118">118:118</a> Thou hast despised all them that fall off from thy judgments; for their thought is unjust. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:119">118:119</a> I have accounted all the sinners of the earth prevaricators: therefore have I loved thy testimonies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:120">118:120</a> Pierce thou my flesh with thy fear: for I am afraid of thy judgments.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:121">118:121</a> [AIN] I have done judgment and justice: give me not up to them that slander me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:122">118:122</a> Uphold thy servant unto good: let not the proud calumniate me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:123">118:123</a> My eyes have fainted after thy salvation: and for the word of thy justice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:124">118:124</a> Deal with thy servant according to thy mercy: and teach me thy justifications. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:125">118:125</a> I am thy servant: give me understanding that I may know thy testimonies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:126">118:126</a> It is time, O Lord, to do: they have dissipated thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:127">118:127</a> Therefore have I loved thy commandments above gold and the topaz. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:128">118:128</a> Therefore was I directed to all thy commandments: I have hated all wicked ways.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:129">118:129</a> [PHE] Thy testimonies are wonderful: therefore my soul hath sought them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:130">118:130</a> The declaration of thy words giveth light: and giveth understanding to little ones. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:131">118:131</a> I opened my mouth and panted: because I longed for thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:132">118:132</a> Look thou upon me, and have mercy on me, according to the judgment of them that love thy name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:133">118:133</a> Direct my steps according to thy word: and let no iniquity have dominion over me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:134">118:134</a> Redeem me from the calumnies of men: that I may keep thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:135">118:135</a> Make thy face to shine upon thy servant: and teach me thy justifications. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:136">118:136</a> My eyes have sent forth springs of water: because they have not kept thy law.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:137">118:137</a> [SADE] Thou art just, O Lord: and thy judgment is right. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:138">118:138</a> Thou hast commanded justice thy testimonies: and thy truth exceedingly. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:139">118:139</a> My zeal hath made me pine away: because my enemies forgot thy words. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:140">118:140</a> Thy word is exceedingly refined: and thy servant hath loved it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:141">118:141</a> I am very young and despised; but I forgot not thy justifications. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:142">118:142</a> Thy justice is justice for ever: and thy law is the truth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:143">118:143</a> Trouble and anguish have found me: thy commandments are my meditation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:144">118:144</a> Thy testimonies are justice for ever: give me understanding, and I shall live.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:145">118:145</a> [COPH] I cried with my whole heart, hear me, O Lord: I will seek thy justifications. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:146">118:146</a> I cried unto thee, save me: that I may keep thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:147">118:147</a> I prevented the dawning of the day, and cried: because in thy words I very much hoped. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:148">118:148</a> My eyes to thee have prevented the morning: that I might meditate on thy words. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:149">118:149</a> Hear thou my voice, O Lord, according to thy mercy: and quicken me according to thy mercy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:150">118:150</a> They that persecute me have drawn nigh to iniquity; but they are gone far off from the law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:151">118:151</a> Thou art near, O Lord: and all thy ways are truth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:152">118:152</a> I have known from the beginning concerning thy testimonies: that thou hast founded them for ever.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:153">118:153</a> [RES] See my humiliation and deliver me: for I have not forgotten the law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:154">118:154</a> Judge my judgment and redeem me: quicken thou me for thy word's sake. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:155">118:155</a> Salvation is far from sinners; because they have not sought thy justifications. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:156">118:156</a> Many, O Lord, are thy mercies: quicken me according to thy judgment. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:157">118:157</a> Many are they that persecute me, and afflict me; but I have not declined from thy testimonies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:158">118:158</a> I beheld the transgressors, and I pined away; because they kept not thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:159">118:159</a> Behold I have loved thy commandments, O Lord; quicken me thou in thy mercy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:160">118:160</a> The beginning of thy words is truth: all the judgments of thy justice are for ever.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:161">118:161</a> [SIN] Princes have persecuted me without cause: and my heart hath been in awe of thy words. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:162">118:162</a> I will rejoice at thy words, as one that hath found great spoil. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:163">118:163</a> I have hated and abhorred iniquity; but I have loved thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:164">118:164</a> Seven times a day I have given praise to thee, for the judgments of thy justice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:165">118:165</a> Much peace have they that love thy law, and to them there is no stumbling block </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:166">118:166</a> I looked to thy salvation, O Lord: and I loved thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:167">118:167</a> My soul hath kept thy testimonies: and hath loved them exceedingly. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:168">118:168</a> I have kept thy commandments and thy testimonies: because all my ways are in thy sight.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:169">118:169</a> [TAU] Let my supplication, O Lord, come near in thy sight: give me understanding according to thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:170">118:170</a> Let my request come in before thee; deliver thou me according to thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:171">118:171</a> My lips shall utter a hymn, when thou shalt teach me thy justifications. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:172">118:172</a> My tongue shall pronounce thy word: because all thy commandments are justice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:173">118:173</a> Let thy hand be with me to save me; for I have chosen thy precepts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:174">118:174</a> I have longed for thy salvation, O Lord; and thy law is my meditation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:175">118:175</a> My soul shall live and shall praise thee: and thy judgments shall help me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:176">118:176</a> I have gone astray like a sheep that is lost: seek thy servant, because I have not forgotten thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:1">119:1</a> In my trouble I cried to the Lord: and he heard me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:2">119:2</a> O Lord, deliver my soul from wicked lips, and a deceitful tongue. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:3">119:3</a> What shall be given to thee, or what shall be added to thee, to a deceitful tongue. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:4">119:4</a> The sharp arrows of the mighty, with coals that lay waste. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:5">119:5</a> Woe is me, that my sojourning is prolonged! I have dwelt with the inhabitants of cedar: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:6">119:6</a> my soul hath been long a sojourner. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:7">119:7</a> With them that hate peace I was peaceable: when I spoke to them they fought against me without cause. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:1">120:1</a> I have lifted up my eyes to the mountains, from whence help shall come to me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:2">120:2</a> My help is from the Lord, who made heaven and earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:3">120:3</a> May he not suffer thy foot to be moved: neither let him slumber that keepeth thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:4">120:4</a> Behold he shall neither slumber nor sleep, that keepeth Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:5">120:5</a> The Lord is thy keeper, the Lord is thy protection upon thy right hand. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:6">120:6</a> The sun shall not burn thee by day: nor the moon by night. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:7">120:7</a> The Lord keepeth thee from all evil: may the Lord keep thy soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:8">120:8</a> May the Lord keep thy going in and thy going out; from henceforth now and for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:1">121:1</a> I rejoiced at the things that were said to me: We shall go into the house of the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:2">121:2</a> Our feet were standing in thy courts, O Jerusalem. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:3">121:3</a> Jerusalem, which is built as a city, which is compact together. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:4">121:4</a> For thither did the tribes go up, the tribes of the Lord: the testimony of Israel, to praise the name of the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:5">121:5</a> Because their seats have sat in judgment, seats upon the house of David. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:6">121:6</a> Pray ye for the things that are for the peace of Jerusalem: and abundance for them that love thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:7">121:7</a> Let peace be in thy strength: and abundance in thy towers. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:8">121:8</a> For the sake of my brethren, and of my neighbours, I spoke peace of thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:9">121:9</a> Because of the house of the Lord our God, I have sought good things for thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:1">122:1</a> To thee have I lifted up my eyes, who dwellest in heaven. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:2">122:2</a> Behold as the eyes of the servants are on the hands of their masters, As the eyes of the handmaid are on the hands of her mistress: so are our eyes unto the Lord our God, until he have mercy on us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:3">122:3</a> Have mercy on us, O Lord, have mercy on us: for we are greatly filled with contempt. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:4">122:4</a> For our soul is greatly filled: we are a reproach to the rich, and contempt to the proud. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:1">123:1</a> If it had not been that the Lord was with us, let Israel now say: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:2">123:2</a> If it had not been that the Lord was with us, When men rose up against us </p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:3">123:3</a> perhaps they had swallowed us up alive. When their fury was enkindled against us, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:4">123:4</a> perhaps the waters had swallowed us up. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:5">123:5</a> Our soul hath passed through a torrent: perhaps our soul had passed through a water insupportable. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:6">123:6</a> Blessed be the Lord, who hath not given us to be a prey to their teeth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:7">123:7</a> Our soul hath been delivered as a sparrow out of the snare of the followers. The snare is broken, and we are delivered. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:8">123:8</a> Our help is in the name of the Lord, who made heaven and earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:1">124:1</a> They that trust in the Lord shall be as mount Sion: he shall not be moved for ever that dwelleth </p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:2">124:2</a> in Jerusalem. Mountains are round about it: so the Lord is round about his people from henceforth now and for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:3">124:3</a> For the Lord will not leave the rod of sinners upon the lot of the just: that the just may not stretch forth their hands to iniquity. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:4">124:4</a> Do good, O Lord, to those that are good, and to the upright of heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:5">124:5</a> But such as turn aside into bonds, the Lord shall lead out with the workers of iniquity: peace upon Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:1">125:1</a> When the lord brought back the captivity of Sion, we became like men comforted. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:2">125:2</a> Then was our mouth filled with gladness; and our tongue with joy. Then shall they say among the Gentiles: The Lord hath done great things for them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:3">125:3</a> The Lord hath done great things for us: we are become joyful. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:4">125:4</a> Turn again our captivity, O Lord, as a stream in the south. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:5">125:5</a> They that sow in tears shall reap in joy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:6">125:6</a> Going they went and wept, casting their seeds. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:7">125:7</a> But coming they shall come with joyfulness, carrying their sheaves. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:1">126:1</a> Unless the Lord build the house, they labour in vain that build it. Unless the Lord keep the city, he watcheth in vain that keepeth it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:2">126:2</a> It is vain for you to rise before light, rise ye after you have sitten, you that eat the bread of sorrow. When he shall give sleep to his beloved, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:3">126:3</a> behold the inheritance of the Lord are children: the reward, the fruit of the womb. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:4">126:4</a> As arrows in the hand of the mighty, so the children of them that have been shaken. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:5">126:5</a> Blessed is the man that hath filled the desire with them; he shall not be confounded when he shall speak to his enemies in the gate. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:1">127:1</a> Blessed are all they that fear the Lord: that walk in his ways. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:2">127:2</a> For thou shalt eat the labours of thy hands: blessed art thou, and it shall be well with thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:3">127:3</a> Thy wife as a fruitful vine, on the sides of thy house. Thy children as olive plants, round about thy table. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:4">127:4</a> Behold, thus shall the man be blessed that feareth the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:5">127:5</a> May the Lord bless thee out of Sion: and mayest thou see the good things of Jerusalem all the days of thy life. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:6">127:6</a> And mayest thou see thy children's children, peace upon Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:1">128:1</a> Often have they fought against me from my youth, let Israel now say. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:2">128:2</a> Often have they fought against me from my youth: but they could not prevail over me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:3">128:3</a> The wicked have wrought upon my back: they have lengthened their iniquity. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:4">128:4</a> The Lord who is just will cut the necks of sinners: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:5">128:5</a> let them all be confounded and turned back that hate Sion. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:6">128:6</a> Let them be as grass on the tops of houses: which withered before it be plucked up: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:7">128:7</a> Wherewith the mower filleth not his hand: nor he that gathereth sheaves his bosom. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:8">128:8</a> And they that have passed by have not said: The blessing of the Lord be upon you: we have blessed you in the name of the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:1">129:1</a> Out of the depths I have cried to thee, O Lord: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:2">129:2</a> Lord, hear my voice. Let thy ears be attentive to the voice of my supplication. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:3">129:3</a> If thou, O Lord, wilt mark iniquities: Lord, who shall stand it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:4">129:4</a> For with thee there is merciful forgiveness: and by reason of thy law, I have waited for thee, O Lord. My soul hath relied on his word: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:5">129:5</a> my soul hath hoped in the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:6">129:6</a> From the morning watch even until night, let Israel hope in the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:7">129:7</a> Because with the Lord there is mercy: and with him plentiful redemption. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:8">129:8</a> And he shall redeem Israel from all his iniquities. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:1">130:1</a> Lord, my heart is not exalted: nor are my eyes lofty. Neither have I walked in great matters, nor in wonderful things above me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:2">130:2</a> If I was not humbly minded, but exalted my soul: As a child that is weaned is towards his mother, so reward in my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:3">130:3</a> Let Israel hope in the Lord, from henceforth now and for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:1">131:1</a> O Lord, remember David, and all his meekness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:2">131:2</a> How he swore to the Lord, he vowed a vow to the God of Jacob: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:3">131:3</a> If I shall enter into the tabernacle of my house: if I shall go up into the bed wherein I lie: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:4">131:4</a> If I shall give sleep to my eyes, or slumber to my eyelids, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:5">131:5</a> Or rest to my temples: until I find out a place for the Lord, a tabernacle for the God of Jacob. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:6">131:6</a> Behold we have heard of it in Ephrata: we have found it in the fields of the wood. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:7">131:7</a> We will go into his tabernacle: We will adore in the place where his feet stood. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:8">131:8</a> Arise, O Lord, into thy resting place: thou and the ark, which thou hast sanctified. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:9">131:9</a> Let thy priests be clothed with justice: and let thy saints rejoice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:10">131:10</a> For thy servant David's sake, turn not away the face of thy anointed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:11">131:11</a> The Lord hath sworn truth to David, and he will not make it void: of the fruit of thy womb I will set upon thy throne. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:12">131:12</a> If thy children will keep thy covenant, and these my testimonies which I shall teach them: Their children also for evermore shall sit upon thy throne. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:13">131:13</a> For the Lord hath chosen Sion: he hath chosen it for his dwelling. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:14">131:14</a> This is my rest for ever and ever: here will I dwell, for I have chosen it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:15">131:15</a> Blessing, I will bless her widow: I will satisfy her poor with bread. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:16">131:16</a> I will clothe her priests with salvation: and her saints shall rejoice with exceeding great joy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:17">131:17</a> There will I bring forth a horn to David: I have prepared a lamp for my anointed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:18">131:18</a> His enemies I will clothe with confusion: but upon him will my sanctification flourish. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:1">132:1</a> Behold how good and how pleasant it is for brethren to dwell in unity. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:2">132:2</a> Like the precious ointment on the head, that ran down upon the beard, the beard of Aaron, Which ran down to the skirt of his garment: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:3">132:3</a> as the dew of Hermon, which descendeth upon mount Sion. For there the Lord hath commandeth blessing, and life for evermore. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_133:1">133:1</a> Behold now bless ye the Lord, all ye servants of the Lord: Who stand in the house of the Lord, in the courts of the house of our God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_133:2">133:2</a> In the nights lift up your hands to the holy places, and bless ye the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_133:3">133:3</a> May the Lord out of Sion bless thee, he that made heaven and earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:1">134:1</a> Praise ye the name of the Lord: O you his servants, praise the Lord: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:2">134:2</a> You that stand in the house of the Lord, in the courts of the house of our God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:3">134:3</a> Praise ye the Lord, for the Lord is good: sing ye to his name, for it is sweet. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:4">134:4</a> For the Lord hath chosen Jacob unto himself: Israel for his own possession. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:5">134:5</a> For I have known that the Lord is great, and our God is above all gods. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:6">134:6</a> Whatsoever the Lord hath pleased he hath done, in heaven, in earth, in the sea, and in all the deeps. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:7">134:7</a> He bringeth up clouds from the end of the earth: he hath made lightnings for the rain. He bringeth forth winds out of his stores: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:8">134:8</a> He slew the firstborn of Egypt from man even unto beast. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:9">134:9</a> He sent forth signs and wonders in the midst of thee, O Egypt: upon Pharao, and upon all his servants. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:10">134:10</a> He smote many nations, and slew mighty kings: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:11">134:11</a> Sehon king of the Amorrhites, and Og king of Basan, and all the kingdoms of Chanaan. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:12">134:12</a> And gave their land for an inheritance, for an inheritance to his people Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:13">134:13</a> Thy name, O Lord, is for ever: thy memorial, O Lord, unto all generations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:14">134:14</a> For the Lord will judge his people, and will be entreated in favour of his servants. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:15">134:15</a> The idols of the Gentiles are silver and gold, the works of men's hands. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:16">134:16</a> They have a mouth, but they speak not: they have eyes, but they see not. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:17">134:17</a> They have ears, but they hear not: neither is there any breath in their mouths. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:18">134:18</a> Let them that make them be like to them: and every one that trusteth in them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:19">134:19</a> Bless the Lord, O house of Israel: bless the Lord, O house of Aaron. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:20">134:20</a> Bless the Lord, O house of Levi: you that fear the Lord, bless the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:21">134:21</a> Blessed be the Lord out of Sion, who dwelleth in Jerusalem. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:1">135:1</a> Praise the Lord, for he is good: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:2">135:2</a> Praise ye the God of gods: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:3">135:3</a> Praise ye the Lord of lords: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:4">135:4</a> Who alone doth great wonders: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:5">135:5</a> Who made the heavens in understanding: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:6">135:6</a> Who established the earth above the waters: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:7">135:7</a> Who made the great lights: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:8">135:8</a> The sun to rule over the day: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:9">135:9</a> The moon and the stars to rule the night: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:10">135:10</a> Who smote Egypt with their firstborn: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:11">135:11</a> Who brought Israel from among them: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:12">135:12</a> With a mighty hand and a stretched out arm: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:13">135:13</a> Who divided the Red Sea into parts: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:14">135:14</a> And brought out Israel through the midst thereof: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:15">135:15</a> And overthrew Pharao and his host in the Red Sea: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:16">135:16</a> Who led his people through the desert: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:17">135:17</a> Who smote great kings: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:18">135:18</a> And slew strong kings: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:19">135:19</a> Sehon king of the Amorrhites: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:20">135:20</a> And Og king of Basan: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:21">135:21</a> And he gave their land for an inheritance: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:22">135:22</a> For an inheritance to his servant Israel: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:23">135:23</a> For he was mindful of us in our affliction: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:24">135:24</a> And he redeemed us from our enemies: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:25">135:25</a> Who giveth food to all flesh: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:26">135:26</a> Give glory to the God of heaven: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:27">135:27</a> Give glory to the Lord of lords: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:1">136:1</a> Upon the rivers of Babylon, there we sat and wept: when we remembered Sion: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:2">136:2</a> On the willows in the midst thereof we hung up our instruments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:3">136:3</a> For there they that led us into captivity required of us the words of songs. And they that carried us away, said: Sing ye to us a hymn of the songs of Sion. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:4">136:4</a> How shall we sing the song of the Lord in a strange land? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:5">136:5</a> If I forget thee, O Jerusalem, let my right hand be forgotten. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:6">136:6</a> Let my tongue cleave to my jaws, if I do not remember thee: If I make not Jerusalem the beginning of my joy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:7">136:7</a> Remember, O Lord, the children of Edom, in the day of Jerusalem: Who say: Rase it, rase it, even to the foundation thereof. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:8">136:8</a> O daughter of Babylon, miserable: blessed shall he be who shall repay thee thy payment which thou hast paid us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:9">136:9</a> Blessed be he that shall take and dash thy little ones against the rock. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:1">137:1</a> I will praise thee, O lord, with my whole heart: for thou hast heard the words of my mouth. I will sing praise to thee in the sight of his angels: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:2">137:2</a> I will worship towards thy holy temple, and I will give glory to thy name. For thy mercy, and for thy truth: for thou hast magnified thy holy name above all. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:3">137:3</a> In what day soever I shall call upon thee, hear me: thou shall multiply strength in my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:4">137:4</a> May all the kings of the earth give glory to thee: for they have heard all the words of thy mouth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:5">137:5</a> And let them sing in the ways of the Lord: for great is the glory of the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:6">137:6</a> For the Lord is high, and looketh on the low: and the high he knoweth afar off. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:7">137:7</a> If I shall walk in the midst of tribulation, thou wilt quicken me: and thou hast stretched forth thy hand against the wrath of my enemies: and thy right hand hath saved me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:8">137:8</a> The Lord will repay for me: thy mercy, O Lord, endureth for ever: O despise not the work of thy hands. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:1">138:1</a> Lord, thou hast proved me, and known me: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:2">138:2</a> thou hast know my sitting down, and my rising up. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:3">138:3</a> Thou hast understood my thoughts afar off: my path and my line thou hast searched out. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:4">138:4</a> And thou hast foreseen all my ways: for there is no speech in my tongue. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:5">138:5</a> Behold, O Lord, thou hast known all things, the last and those of old: thou hast formed me, and hast laid thy hand upon me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:6">138:6</a> Thy knowledge is become wonderful to me: it is high, and I cannot reach to it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:7">138:7</a> Whither shall I go from thy spirit? or whither shall I flee from thy face? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:8">138:8</a> If I ascend into heaven, thou art there: if I descend into hell, thou art present. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:9">138:9</a> If I take my wings early in the morning, and dwell in the uttermost parts of the sea: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:10">138:10</a> Even there also shall thy hand lead me: and thy right hand shall hold me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:11">138:11</a> And I said: Perhaps darkness shall cover me: and night shall be my light in my pleasures. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:12">138:12</a> But darkness shall not be dark to thee, and night shall be light as day: the darkness thereof, and the light thereof are alike to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:13">138:13</a> For thou hast possessed my reins: thou hast protected me from my mother's womb. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:14">138:14</a> I will praise thee, for thou art fearfully magnified: wonderful are thy works, and my soul knoweth right well. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:15">138:15</a> My bone is not hidden from thee, which thou hast made in secret: and my substance in the lower parts of the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:16">138:16</a> Thy eyes did see my imperfect being, and in thy book all shall be written: days shall be formed, and no one in them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:17">138:17</a> But to me thy friends, O God, are made exceedingly honourable: their principality is exceedingly strengthened. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:18">138:18</a> I will number them, and they shall be multiplied above the sand: I rose up and am still with thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:19">138:19</a> If thou wilt kill the wicked, O God: ye men of blood, depart from me: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:20">138:20</a> Because you say in thought: They shall receive thy cities in vain. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:21">138:21</a> Have I not hated them, O Lord, that hated thee: and pine away because of thy enemies? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:22">138:22</a> I have hated them with a perfect hatred: and they are become enemies to me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:23">138:23</a> Prove me, O God, and know my heart: examine me, and know my paths. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:24">138:24</a> And see if there be in me the way of iniquity: and lead me in the eternal way. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:1">139:1</a> Unto the end, a psalm for David. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:2">139:2</a> Deliver me, O Lord, from the evil man: rescue me from the unjust man. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:3">139:3</a> Who have devised iniquities in their hearts: all the day long they designed battles. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:4">139:4</a> They have sharpened their tongues like a serpent: the venom of saps is under their lips. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:5">139:5</a> Keep me, O Lord, from the hand of the wicked: and from unjust men deliver me. Who have proposed to supplant my steps. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:6">139:6</a> the proud have hidden a net for me. And they have stretched out cords for a snare: they have laid for me a stumblingblock by the wayside. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:7">139:7</a> I said to the Lord: Thou art my God: hear, O Lord, the voice of my supplication. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:8">139:8</a> O Lord, Lord, the strength of my salvation: thou hast overshadowed my head in the day of battle. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:9">139:9</a> Give me not up, O Lord, from my desire to the wicked: they have plotted against me; do not thou forsake me, lest they should triumph. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:10">139:10</a> The head of them compassing me about: the labour of their lips shall overwhelm them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:11">139:11</a> Burning coals shall fall upon them; thou wilt cast them down into the fire: in miseries they shall not be able to stand. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:12">139:12</a> A man full of tongue shall not be established in the earth: evil shall catch the unjust man unto destruction. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:13">139:13</a> I know that the Lord will do justice to the needy, and will revenge the poor. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:14">139:14</a> But as for the just, they shall give glory to thy name: and the upright shall dwell with thy countenance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:1">140:1</a> I have cried to the, O Lord, hear me: hearken to my voice, when I cry to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:2">140:2</a> Let my prayer be directed as incense in thy sight; the lifting up of my hands, as evening sacrifice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:3">140:3</a> Set a watch, O Lord, before my mouth: and a door round about my lips. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:4">140:4</a> Incline not my heart to evil words; to make excuses in sins. With men that work iniquity: and I will not communicate with the choicest of them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:5">140:5</a> The just shall correct me in mercy, and shall reprove me: but let not the oil of the sinner fatten my head. For my prayer also shall still be against the things with which they are well pleased: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:6">140:6</a> their judges falling upon the rock have been swallowed up. They shall hear my words, for they have prevailed: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:7">140:7</a> as when the thickness of the earth is broken up upon the ground: Our bones are scattered by the side of hell. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:8">140:8</a> But o to thee, O Lord, Lord, are my eyes: in thee have I put my trust, take not away my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:9">140:9</a> Keep me from the snare, which they have laid for me, and from the stumblingblocks of them that work iniquity. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:10">140:10</a> The wicked shall fall in his net: I am alone until I pass. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:1">141:1</a> Of understanding for David. A prayer when he was in the cave. [1 Kings 24]. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:2">141:2</a> I cried to the Lord with my voice: with my voice I made supplication to the Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:3">141:3</a> In his sight I pour out my prayer, and before him I declare my trouble: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:4">141:4</a> When my spirit failed me, then thou newest my paths. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:5">141:5</a> I looked on my right hand, and beheld, and there was no one that would know me. Flight hath failed me: and there is no one that hath regard to my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:6">141:6</a> I cried to thee, O Lord: I said: Thou art my hope, my portion in the land of the living. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:7">141:7</a> Attend to my supplication: for I am brought very low. Deliver me from my persecutors; for they are stronger than I. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:8">141:8</a> Bring my soul out of prison, that I may praise thy name: the just wait for me, until thou reward me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:1">142:1</a> Hear, O Lord, my prayer: give ear to my supplication in thy truth: hear me in thy justice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:2">142:2</a> And enter not into judgment with thy servant: for in thy sight no man living shall be justified. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:3">142:3</a> For the enemy hath persecuted my soul: he hath brought down my life to the earth. He hath made me to dwell in darkness as those that have been dead of old: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:4">142:4</a> and my spirit is in anguish within me: my heart within me is troubled. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:5">142:5</a> I remembered the days of old, I meditated on all thy works: I meditated upon the works of thy hands. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:6">142:6</a> I stretched forth my hands to thee: my soul is as earth without water unto thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:7">142:7</a> Hear me speedily, O Lord: my spirit hath fainted away. Turn not away thy face from me, lest I be like unto them that go down into the pit. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:8">142:8</a> Cause me to hear thy mercy in the morning; for in thee have I hoped. Make the way known to me, wherein I should walk: for I have lifted up my soul to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:9">142:9</a> Deliver me from my enemies, O Lord, to thee have I fled: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:10">142:10</a> teach me to do thy will, for thou art my God. Thy good spirit shall lead me into the right land: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:11">142:11</a> for thy name's sake, O Lord, thou wilt quicken me in thy justice. Thou wilt bring my soul out of trouble: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:12">142:12</a> and in thy mercy thou wilt destroy my enemies. And thou wilt cut off all them that afflict my soul: for I am thy servant. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:1">143:1</a> Blessed be the Lord my God, who teacheth my hands to fight, and my fingers to war. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:2">143:2</a> My mercy, and my refuge: my support, and my deliverer: My protector, and I have hoped in him: who subdueth my people under me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:3">143:3</a> Lord, what is man, that thou art made known to him? or the son of man, that thou makest account of him? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:4">143:4</a> Man is like to vanity: his days pass away like a shadow. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:5">143:5</a> Lord, bow down thy heavens and descend: touch the mountains and they shall smoke. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:6">143:6</a> Send forth lightning, and thou shalt scatter them: shoot out thy arrows, and thou shalt trouble them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:7">143:7</a> Put forth thy hand from on high, take me out, and deliver me from many waters: from the hand of strange children: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:8">143:8</a> Whose mouth hath spoken vanity: and their right hand is the right hand of iniquity. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:9">143:9</a> To thee, O God, I will sing a new canticle: on the psaltery and an instrument of ten strings I will sing praises to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:10">143:10</a> Who givest salvation to kings: who hast redeemed thy servant David from the malicious sword: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:11">143:11</a> Deliver me, And rescue me out of the hand of strange children; whose mouth hath spoken vanity: and their right hand is the right hand of iniquity: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:12">143:12</a> Whose sons are as new plants in their youth: Their daughters decked out, adorned round about after the similitude of a temple: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:13">143:13</a> Their storehouses full, flowing out of this into that. Their sheep fruitful in young, abounding in their goings forth: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:14">143:14</a> their oxen fat. There is no breach of wall, nor passage, nor crying out in their streets. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:15">143:15</a> They have called the people happy, that hath these things: but happy is that people whose God is the Lord. </p>
