 <p><a name="an_144:1">144:1</a> I will extol thee, O God my king: and I will bless thy name for ever; yea, for ever and ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:2">144:2</a> Every day I will bless thee: and I will praise thy name for ever; yea, for ever and ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:3">144:3</a> Great is the Lord, and greatly to be praised: and of his greatness there is no end. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:4">144:4</a> Generation and generation shall praise thy works: and they shall declare thy power. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:5">144:5</a> They shall speak of the magnificence of the glory of thy holiness: and shall tell thy wondrous works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:6">144:6</a> And they shall speak of the might of thy terrible acts: and shall declare thy greatness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:7">144:7</a> They shall publish the memory of the abundance of thy sweetness: and shall rejoice in thy justice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:8">144:8</a> The Lord is gracious and merciful: patient and plenteous in mercy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:9">144:9</a> The Lord is sweet to all: and his tender mercies are over all his works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:10">144:10</a> Let all thy works, O lord, praise thee: and let thy saints bless thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:11">144:11</a> They shall speak of the glory of thy kingdom: and shall tell of thy power: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:12">144:12</a> To make thy might known to the sons of men: and the glory of the magnificence of thy kingdom. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:13">144:13</a> Thy kingdom is a kingdom of all ages: and thy dominion endureth throughout all generations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:14">144:14</a> The Lord lifteth up all that fall: and setteth up all that are cast down. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:15">144:15</a> The eyes of all hope in thee, O Lord: and thou givest them meat in due season. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:16">144:16</a> Thou openest thy hand, and fillest with blessing every living creature. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:17">144:17</a> The Lord is just in all his ways: and holy in all his works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:18">144:18</a> The Lord is nigh unto all them that call upon him: to all that call upon him in truth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:19">144:19</a> He will do the will of them that fear him: and he will hear their prayer, and save them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:20">144:20</a> The Lord keepeth all them that love him; but all the wicked he will destroy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:21">144:21</a> My mouth shall speak the praise of the Lord: and let all flesh bless thy holy name for ever; yea, for ever and ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:1">145:1</a> Alleluia, of Aggeus and Zacharias. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:2">145:2</a> Praise the Lord, O my soul, in my life I will praise the Lord: I will sing to my God as long as I shall be. Put not your trust in princes: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:3">145:3</a> in the children of men, in whom there is no salvation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:4">145:4</a> His spirit shall go forth, and he shall return into his earth: in that day all their thoughts shall perish. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:5">145:5</a> Blessed is he who hath the God of Jacob for his helper, whose hope is in the Lord his God: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:6">145:6</a> who made heaven and earth, the sea, and all things that are in them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:7">145:7</a> Who keepeth truth for ever: who executeth judgment for them that suffer wrong: who giveth food to the hungry. The Lord looseth them that are fettered: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:8">145:8</a> the Lord enlighteneth the blind. The Lord lifteth up them that are cast down: the Lord loveth the just. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:9">145:9</a> The Lord keepeth the strangers, he will support the fatherless and the widow: and the ways of sinners he will destroy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:10">145:10</a> The Lord shall reign for ever: thy God, O Sion, unto generation and generation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:1">146:1</a> Praise ye the Lord, because psalm is good: to our God be joyful and comely praise. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:2">146:2</a> The Lord buildeth up Jerusalem: he will gather together the dispersed of Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:3">146:3</a> Who healeth the broken of heart, and bindeth up their bruises. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:4">146:4</a> Who telleth the number of the stars: and calleth them all by their names. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:5">146:5</a> Great is our Lord, and great is his power: and of his wisdom there is no number. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:6">146:6</a> The Lord lifteth up the meek, and bringeth the wicked down even to the ground. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:7">146:7</a> Sing ye to the Lord with praise: sing to our God upon the harp. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:8">146:8</a> Who covereth the heaven with clouds, and prepareth rain for the earth. Who maketh grass to grow on the mountains, and herbs for the service of men. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:9">146:9</a> Who giveth to beasts their food: and to the young ravens that call upon him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:10">146:10</a> He shall not delight in the strength of the horse: nor take pleasure in the legs of a man. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:11">146:11</a> The Lord taketh pleasure in them that fear him: and in them that hope in his mercy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:12">147:12</a> Praise the Lord, O Jerusalem: praise thy God, O Sion. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:13">147:13</a> Because he hath strengthened the bolts of thy gates, he hath blessed thy children within thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:14">147:14</a> Who hath placed peace in thy borders: and filleth thee with the fat of corn. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:15">147:15</a> Who sendeth forth his speech to the earth: his word runneth swiftly. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:16">147:16</a> Who giveth snow like wool: scattereth mists like ashes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:17">147:17</a> He sendeth his crystal like morsels: who shall stand before the face of his cold? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:18">147:18</a> He shall send out his word, and shall melt them: his wind shall blow, and the waters shall run. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:19">147:19</a> Who declareth his word to Jacob: his justices and his judgments to Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:20">147:20</a> He hath not done in like manner to every nation: and his judgments he hath not made manifest to them. Alleluia. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:1">148:1</a> Praise ye the Lord from the heavens: praise ye him in the high places. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:2">148:2</a> Praise ye him , all his angels: praise ye him, all his hosts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:3">148:3</a> Praise ye him, O sun and moon: praise him, all ye stars and light. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:4">148:4</a> Praise him, ye heavens of heavens: and let all the waters that are above the heavens </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:5">148:5</a> praise the name of the Lord. For he spoke, and they were made: he commanded, and they were created. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:6">148:6</a> He hath established them for ever, and for ages of ages: he hath made a decree, and it shall not pass away. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:7">148:7</a> Praise the Lord from the earth, ye dragons, and all ye deeps: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:8">148:8</a> Fire, hail, snow, ice, stormy winds which fulfil his word: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:9">148:9</a> Mountains and all hills, fruitful trees and all cedars: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:10">148:10</a> Beasts and all cattle: serpents and feathered fowls: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:11">148:11</a> Kings of the earth and all people: princes and all judges of the earth: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:12">148:12</a> Young men and maidens: let the old with the younger, praise the name of the Lord: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:13">148:13</a> for his name alone is exalted. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:14">148:14</a> The praise of him is above heaven and earth: and he hath exalted the horn of his people. A hymn to all his saints: to the children of Israel, a people approaching to him. Alleluia. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:1">149:1</a> Sing ye to the Lord a new canticle: let his praise be in the church of the saints. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:2">149:2</a> Let Israel rejoice in him that made him: and let the children of Sion be joyful in their king. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:3">149:3</a> Let them praise his name in choir: let them sing to him with the timbrel and the psaltery. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:4">149:4</a> For the Lord is well pleased with his people: and he will exalt the meek unto salvation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:5">149:5</a> The saints shall rejoice in glory: they shall be joyful in their beds. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:6">149:6</a> The high praise of God shall be in their mouth: and two-edged swords in their hands: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:7">149:7</a> To execute vengeance upon the nations, chastisements among the people: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:8">149:8</a> To bind their kings with fetters, and their nobles with manacles of iron. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:9">149:9</a> To execute upon them the judgment that is written: this glory is to all his saints. Alleluia. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:1">150:1</a> Praise ye the Lord in his holy places: praise ye him in the firmament of his power. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:2">150:2</a> Praise ye him for his mighty acts: praise ye him according to the multitude of his greatness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:3">150:3</a> Praise him with sound of trumpet: praise him with psaltery and harp. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:4">150:4</a> Praise him with timbrel and choir: praise him with strings and organs. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:5">150:5</a> Praise him on high sounding cymbals: praise him on cymbals of joy: let every spirit praise the Lord. Alleluia.</p> 
 <p></p><hr>
